Inside the cave, the atmosphere was a pale misty yellow. It seemed to be some toxic mist.

Ziya took caution to their surroundings and created a protective space around Geoffrey to keep him from the poisonous mist with a swift wave of his hand.

Buzz! After exercising the Space Godly Way successfully, Ziya was lost in his thoughts for a moment before he muttered to himself, "It seems the basic Godly Ways also work here…"

The three thousand Godly Ways were derived from the Ways-blending Energy, which was also the foundation of the chaos.

If there was no trace of Ways-blending Energy in this world, the three thousand Godly Ways would refuse to exist. As a result, Ziya would be rendered powerless as he would fail to display the power of any Godly Way.

"Alright then, let's head inside and take a closer look!"

The deeper they went into the cave, the more excited Ziya got to explore what lay inside of it. Giving in to his enthusiastic self, Ziya grabbed ahold of Geoffrey's arm and dragged him along to move faster. The next moment, the two of them morphed into individual beams of light that rushed their way into the depths of the cave.

Initially, Ziya had imagined the cave to be similar to any average cave he had come across. He thought if they rushed through, it wouldn't take long before they would reach the other side. But after hundreds of miles of travel, the space ahead would refuse to meet any end and would just appear to get wider and wider. Moreover, the yellow poisonous mist didn't seem to subside even after coming this far.

"This world appears to be quite peculiar. Geoffrey, stand firm and maintain a good grip!"

Just as he exclaimed his instructions, Ziya employed the Grand Teleportation technique and disappeared from the spot he once stood along with Geoffrey.

Buzz! Using this ability, Ziya was able to cover a great distance of more than ten million miles each time without a hitch.

Soon after, Ziya and Geoffrey found themselves in another space. This one was much wider than the last, and they weren't even able to locate the surrounding edges due to how spacious it was. In terms of appearance, it resembled the chaos with only one visible exception; the air wasn't decorated with chaotic clouds scattered about, but it had the yellow poisonous mist they had encountered earlier.

"This place holds a striking resemblance to the chaos, doesn't it?" Geoffrey asked as he looked around to soak in his surroundings.

He had never seen the chaos with his own eyes before. The only source of information he had was through various descriptions he had heard in the past regarding it.

"No, not really," Ziya shook his head to disregard Geoffrey's statement and continued, "It's just a larger cave than the one we were previously in. This world is quite strange. It seems to be made up of countless gigantic caves that cease to end. It could be said that this is a world of caves..."

As he spoke, Ziya gripped Geoffrey's hand firmly once more and used the Grand Teleportation technique over and over again.

Just like the previous times, they teleported to another vast cave, and just like the others, it was desolate with no signs of life anywhere. Except for the constant yellow poisonous mist that followed them everywhere, they never found anything else that appealed to their interests.

After more than a hundred successive implementations of the Grand Teleportation technique, they entered the vicinity of a new cave.

However, this time, they finally found something worth a second glance. At the bottom of this cave, there was a layer of huge pits like volcano craters closely packed against each other.

"Wow! There are so many volcanoes down there…" Geoffrey exclaimed in a high-pitched tone out of overflowing excitement. His eyes gleamed with joy.

"They aren't volcanoes," Ziya rubbed his chin as he squinted his eyes to look into the distance. "It seems they are lairs of some creatures that live down there."

Ziya had dragged Geoffrey along a great distance. Geoffrey was only able to comprehend the many caves flashing by his eyes when they teleported, but all this while Ziya had spread his spiritual sense in his surroundings to keep a lookout at all times.

With his observational skills, he had already found some clues and began to conceptualize a theory about this world.

In the depths of these huge caves, there were subtle traces of living beings, and even ruins of some simple buildings that had been buried deep underground for a very long time.

Even the sturdiest of buildings couldn't bear through the erosion of time and collapsed under pressure. After the passing of one or ten billion years, everything would eventually be reduced to nothing but soil.

However, this place was quite different. Ziya had sensed life force coming from those volcano craters. He instantly pinned them to be living creatures.

As soon as the two of them made their way to the ground, they noticed a fountain of yellow poisonous mist spurt out uncontrollably from a volcano crater within close proximity. As if on cue, brownish-yellow four-legged snakes slithered their way out of the mist and dashed towards them intending to kill.

These four-legged snakes appeared to be quite hostile with a malicious aura surrounding them. Their backs were covered in dense yellow poison sacs.

Their fearful appearance made Geoffrey feel intimidated by them as he subconsciously froze in place.

With a click of his tongue, Ziya expressed his disappointment as he shook his head and said, "Don't be scared. They're low-level creatures who lack intelligence."

As he spoke, he stretched out a hand and pressed it in the air. Long swords appeared out of nowhere and nailed these four-legged snakes down to the ground, killing them instantly.

"I can't believe there's no intelligent creatures in this world. We need to keep looking for them!"

Ziya fell in utter dismay as to what might have happened to this world.

However, if there existed any Other Shore Realm or Eternal Realm masters, they might have left some traces in this world to vouch for their existence.

Buzz! Buzz! Buzz! Buzz! Ziya used the Grand Teleportation technique over and over again.

After countless attempts, Geoffrey suddenly reminded him, "Master Ziya, if the Finale Way also existed in this world and it already failed, then no intelligent creatures would exist after that. Am I right?"

Hearing Geoffrey's words, Ziya stopped during the course of his action of using the Grand Teleportation technique and was stunned into silence.

When every round of chaos came to an end, everything in the world would be eliminated, leaving no traces of lives whatsoever.

Could it be that this world had been completely destroyed after the Finale Way failed? Chapter 3843 Investigation Geoffrey's words put into the light the current situation of this world to Ziya.

When a round of chaos ended, a destructive power would eliminate everything in the entire world.

After that, if no new intelligent lives managed to be birthed, then the world would exist as nothing more than a shell.

Ziya nodded. "You're right. Maybe the Purge Way and the Nihility Way also existed in this world and the ones who believed in the latter dominated everyone and destroyed everything. Or maybe the Purge Way won. They limited the number of creatures in a very small range and hid themselves somewhere in these caves."

This world was infinitely vast and trying to locate that small number of creatures was even more difficult than finding a needle in a haystack.

Either way, they knew the Finale Way in this world had failed.

"Is there also an Other Shore in this world?" Geoffrey asked. Ziya couldn't help but raise an eyebrow at Geoffrey's question.

"It's possible. Why not come with me to see if there is one!"

Since the three thousand Godly Ways worked in this world then the Truths of Godly Ways must be the same since they were derived from the Instant Civilization, a far more superior civilization from the Abstruse Energy World.

They should be more universal than the Ways-blending Energy.

Geoffrey had completely mastered the Truth of Cultivation Nature under the Regal Jade Spirit's guidance, however, Zen never allowed him to leave his inner world. He still hadn't even gotten the chance to enter the Sea of Truth, yet here was Ziya inviting him to explore the Other Shore of this strange world.

Buzz! In a flash, Ziya sat cross-legged in the air and clapped four consecutive times in all directions. Four palm shadows appeared around him that held faint sword shadows. These sword shadows slowly rotated around him and Geoffrey protectively.

This world seemed devoid of all lives but it was never unwise to carry a bit of protection.

The two of them then began to recite the Truths of Godly Ways and tried to enter the Other Shore.

Slowly, the yellow, poisonous mist around the area headed towards them.

Soon enough, the two of them were surrounded by it.

A trace of curiosity appeared on Ziya's face. "Can the Truths of Godly Ways attract the poisonous mist?"

Back when they cultivated the Truths of Godly Ways in the chaos, they never attracted chaotic energy like this. Then again, this world was vastly different from the chaos.

As the two of them continued to recite, the whole world began to spin around them.

Newcomers to the Other Shore of the chaos would first arrive in the Sea of Truth but subsequent visits would lead them to the exact spot of their last exit.

A thin figure popped out from behind him. He was the black-haired teenager, Usman.

A hint of madness flashed in his eyes. As soon as he jumped off, he rushed towards a gigantic flying ship like an arrow.

"I'm going to tear this ship apart!"

For some reason, he looked oddly excited, and his heart hammered in his chest.

Although he could previously kill people at will, those he had fought before were people the Ji Clan had selected. Once they fought to a certain extent, they were forced to fall asleep, and Usman felt that it wasn't exciting at all.

Now, he finally had the chance to kill on his own accord.

He flew directly towards the giant flying ship and sensed a large number of people's breaths in it. To tear the flying ship apart was naturally the most efficient way to kill them.

"How dare you!" Pearce screamed.

His face darkened, and he froze as if the frost had enveloped him.

Then, his right hand shook violently, and a handful of blood mist gushed out of his right arm. The blood mist condensed quickly and turned into a long sword.

"God-detaining Sword! Go to hell!"

"Buzz!"

The sword moved so swiftly in zigzag motions, and then it slashed at Usman's front.

"Puff!"

There seemed to be only the giant flying ship in Usman's eyes. As Pearce went all-out with his sword attack, he did not dodge. Instead, he withstood the strike with his physical body.

The powerful sword radiance left a mark on Usman's body, but the mark only lasted for a few seconds before it disappeared.

"This young man isn't at the Chaotic Source Realm.

But he can withstand my full blow! How is that possible?" said Pearce.

He couldn't believe his eyes! If Usman was at the Chaotic Source Realm, then it was understandable that he could block his sword strike, but he was not! The sword radiance clearly left a trace just now, but it disappeared quickly.

How could someone who wasn't at the Chaotic Source Realm withstand his blow? He suddenly felt that the world had gotten even more mysterious. Some young men who appeared out of nowhere looked quite exceptional, and their strengths were simply beyond his imagination. Zen and Usman who was in front of him, were included.

"Stop him!"

Just then, three evil eyes floated out of Auden's body and released countless sharp swords.

The sharp swords stabbed Usman's body, but their effect was just the same as Pearce's attack. They left multiple scars on Usman, but they were small, shallow, and healed immediately.

"Go to hell!"

"Boom!"

The whole giant flying ship shook violently, and the disciples of the Oneness Sky Palace inside also tumbled due to the sudden movement.

Light shone inside the ship through the cracks. The disciples of the Oneness Sky Palace inside the cabin blanched with fear. They all thought that they would be safe inside the flying ship, but they never expected for such a disaster to happen.

Beads of sweat rolled down their temples. They saw through the crack that there was a boy in his teens outside the ship.

Even though the boy was just a teen, no one dared to come forward! Just as everyone was about to retreat, a quick figure already dashed towards the crack.

It was Libby whose long legs tapped lightly on the ground, and she left a shadow every time she touched the floor.

When she was near Usman, she lifted the long sword and shook her right hand at the same time.

"Chill Rope!"

In a split second, a rope wrapped around Usman.

"Buzz!"

After the rope had bound his body, it turned into a mark and appeared on his neck.

"Get out!" Libby shouted and swung her sword at him.

Her sword strike had the power of eighteen thousand divine megatons! Usman's excitement only increased as he stared at Libby's angry face. Then, he stretched out his hand and casually tried to grab Libby's sword.

Eighteen thousand divine megatons of power was indeed not enough to defeat him.

After Pearce and the other mighty warriors of the Oneness Sky Palace had attacked him, he was still unharmed.

However, he was slightly shocked when he touched Libby's sword.

It turned out that the sword's power had suddenly increased by three times and reached a total of fifty-four thousand divine megatons! His abilities allowed him to resist the power that was ten times stronger than fifty-four thousand divine megatons of force.

Yet, he knew nothing about the Chill Rope. While the rope secured him tightly, the power of all Libby's attacks was multiplied by three times. Of course, the sudden increase caught him off-guard.

"Bang, bang!"

Even in the face of an invincible opponent, Libby wasn't afraid at all. She had always focused on cultivating the sword skill as a diligent disciple of the Oneness Sky Palace. She had done her best to improve, and little by little became so powerful.

After that, a long sword followed behind Usman like a shadow.

The blade the space had formed immediately spread out.

"Crack!"

Everything happened so quickly. It was as if an invisible blade moved past and cut the flying ship in two with a crisp sound.

Chapter 3848 High In The Sky The invisible space blade, after cutting open the huge flying ship, continued to expand in all directions.

Chapter 3850 Challenge Usman hadn't fully grown up yet, so he was still much weaker than his previous self in the past.

Chapter 3851 Tomos A hint of fear could be seen in Yellow Thearch's eyes.

The Element Spirit race didn't extend their help and support for free, and it was now time for them to pay the price.

Whoosh! The golden light soared into the sky and then began to pour down.

It was as if someone had pierced through the sun with a sword and caused the flames to flow down the sun's body.

But that wasn't a flame. It was the holy way, a comprehension exclusive to Yellow Thearch.

"Good timing!"

Fuxi exclaimed, his face lighting up.

He trembled with excitement, not having met an opponent of this level in a long time.

The golden holy path poured down, an inexplicable aura surrounding it.

The weaker disciples of the Oneness Sky Palace bent down to kneel before the holy path.

It took a lot of energy even for powerful and strong-minded warriors like Libby to resist the aura.

Buzz! A mark of Eight Diagrams suddenly appeared on the golden holy path.

Fuxi then threw a punch at this mark, a boom resounding through the people present.

Fuxi's punch smashed the invincible and overbearing-looking holy way into pieces.

Whoosh! Fuxi had also disappeared along with the holy path.

But in the next moment, he appeared behind Yellow Thearch, with a mark of Eight Diagrams on Yellow Thearch's back.

"I have disliked you for a long time!" Fuxi said as he prepared to throw a punch.

As long as the mark of Eight Diagrams remained with him, this punch would definitely hit its target.

There were very few people in this world who could resist Fuxi's punch.

Yellow Thearch, who had turned around at Fuxi's words, swung his sword towards Fuxi's fist.

Yellow Thearch would suffer greatly against Fuxi's fist, but if his sword were to pierce into Fuxi's fist, it would disable one of his arms for the time being.

Fuxi frowned and lowered his hand, dodging Yellow Thearch's sword. He wanted to attack him again.

But Yellow Thearch's sword was still aimed at Fuxi's fist after it had drawn a circle.

After a while, it looked like they were sparring with each other. The way they were fighting looked strange and absurd, but they were in great danger.

Fuxi was an irritable man. He retreated a thousand feet in the air, gathering all his energies to throw another punch. But Yellow Thearch merely smiled as he said, "It's too late."

Bang! The mark on Yellow Thearch's back exploded with a loud bang.

The mark of Eight Diagrams lasted for a while and would automatically explode if Fuxi didn't trigger it.

The explosion was powerful enough to be impressive, but it was nothing to Yellow Thearch.

Fuxi looked at Yellow Thearch, his face devoid of expression, and said, "You haven't made any progress over all these years."

"I've made enough to defeat you!"

Yellow Thearch had raised his sword up before him so that it was parallel to the ground. As the golden light boomed again, the two top masters of the Source World dove in to fight each other once again.

Yellow Thearch had just made his move when Divine Farmer made his way across the space to Elizabeth's side, one hand on the red crystal.

Fuxi was very clear about the fact that someone else would be attacking Zen. But he had no choice but to go all out while facing Yellow Thearch.

He'd face defeat if he so much as got distracted one tiny bit. That was why he couldn't protect Zen at the moment.

"Let go of him and I won't kill you," Divine Farmer said, staring at Elizabeth.

The old man was not unfamiliar to Elizabeth.

She had come into contact with Divine Farmer several times when she had followed Emperor Charm. This was how they were familiar with each other.

"I can't do that," Elizabeth said, shrugging.

"So be it. You should know that I'm not going to let you off even if Emperor Charm is still alive," Divine Farmer said, wiggling his hand and causing a jade ruler to pop out of his arm.

The Divine Farmer Ruler was his life's treasure, which could both kill and save people.

He waved the ruler around before throwing a deadly-looking strike at Elizabeth.

It was obvious that the Divine Farmer Ruler was going to kill people. As Divine Farmer waved the ruler around, the smell of blood permeated the air around them. If the weaker ones were to take even one sip, their skin and flesh would rot and they would turn into dried bones.

Now that she was facing an Eternal Realm master who was even stronger than Emperor Charm, Elizabeth didn't know how to fight back.

She lowered her body in order to avoid the Divine Farmer Ruler and moved behind the crystal.

Since Divine Farmer and Elizabeth were previously acquainted, he showed her some mercy. But if he were to use all his strength, he would definitely kill her.

However, after Elizabeth had dodged him by hiding behind the red crystal, the surging divine flames of the Sun Crow race shot towards Divine Farmer along the red crystal, and in an instant, surrounded him.

Phew! The divine flames of the Sun Crow race still couldn't destroy Divine Farmer's Chaotic Source Spirits, but Divine Farmer was angry. "You're reckless, aren't you?" he spat out. "You're courting death!"

Thick green light flashed out from the center of the Divine Farmer Ruler and turned into a green, thumb-sized hummingbird.

The hummingbird devoured the divine flames of the Sun Crow race on the surface of Divine Farmer's body, and then charged towards Elizabeth.

"Venomous Candle Hummingbird!" Elizabeth said knowingly.

She was experienced and knowledgeable, and knew that this theurgy of Divine Farmer was formidable.

If she didn't retreat now, this little hummingbird would definitely kill her.

Whoosh! Elizabeth loosened her grip and entered the space channel, simultaneously appearing at a spot thousands of feet away.

Her eyebrows furrowed in indignation.

The gap between her strength and Divine Farmer's was too great.

It was obvious that she was no match for him.

Divine Farmer was about to move away with the red crystal when a cloud of black smoke suddenly appeared on the surface of the red crystal.

The black smoke had a special characteristic that allowed it to drill into the red crystal.

"Is that the Filthy Smoke?"

Elizabeth was surprised to see the black smoke.

Anything that was tainted with the Filthy Smoke couldn't be transferred through space channels.

Half of Divine Farmer's body had already drilled into the space channel. He didn't know what was happening outside. When he grabbed the red crystal and tried to stuff it into the channel, he discovered that he couldn't do it.

He had no choice but to drill out of the space channel. On inspection, he found that an Ear Mouse was holding a cigarette pipe and blowing out black smoke.

It was none other than Tomos, the betrayer of the Ear Mouse race and a member of the Black Ship.

Chapter 3852 Cooperation According to the Divine Farmer's plan, he must leave with the red crystal as quickly as possible. He must do this without any delay.

He thought that if the captain of the Black Ship tried to stop him, he would immediately release a space snake.

It was known that the space snakes were almost extinct within the Three Purities Stage. They naturally lived in the void. However, there were only three of them left now, one of which was in the possession of the Divine Farmer.

The space snake was given to the Divine Farmer as a gift. He received it from the Element Spirit race.

The space snake had a rare and useful ability. It could temporarily change the shape of the space channel. This was extremely helpful in times when the user wanted to make sure that no one else could enter the space channel.

The Divine Farmer figured that he would be able to escape with Zen as long as the captain of the Black Ship didn't break his space channel.

However, a problem occurred before he could even drag Zen into the space channel. The red crystal had already been contaminated by the Filthy Smoke. The expression on the Divine Farmer's face was indescribable. It looked frightening.

His strength was comparable to that of the Yellow Thearch. However, he preferred not getting into fights. He rarely fought whenever he was in the Source World.

"How dare you stop me?" Anger began to show in the Divine Farmer's eyes. He grabbed the red crystal with his left hand. Meanwhile, he held the Divine Farmer Ruler on his right. With that, he charged fearlessly towards Tomos.

Even though it was now facing an Eternal Realm master, Tomos maintained its composure.

As it saw the Divine Farmer approaching it at breakneck speed, Tomos immediately smoked its pipe.

Bang! A loud noise echoed through the space.

Before Tomos could blow the smoke out of its pipe, the Divine Farmer had already hacked at its head with the ruler.

A direct attack from an Eternal Realm master was more than enough to kill a Holy Soul Realm warrior.

As soon as the Divine Farmer slashed, he easily cracked and split Tomos' skull wide open. Its body appeared as though it had been seared by the scorching sun. In addition to that, it had no shape. There was only some sort of gray smoke under its skin.

Whoosh! Whoosh! As the gray smoke started to dissipate, it quickly formed a cage and effectively trapped the Divine Farmer inside it.

"You are truly extraordinary as an Eternal Realm master. I must admit that I have always admired you. However, I may have to offend you today."

The members of the Black Ship were a little different from other forces. It was in the sense that all of them were desperadoes. The moment they decided to join the Black Ship, they had already abandoned everything else.

They didn't care whether they lived or died.

They didn't care about how powerful their opponents were. No matter what happened, they refused to give up without a fight.

Just then, three Ear Mice that looked exactly like Tomos appeared inside the cage. It was apparent that they were made out of the smoke.

"I'm afraid it would be very unwise of you to provoke me!"

The Divine Farmer slowly raised the green ruler in his hand. As he did this, he lightly stepped into the air.

A string of bright and colorful lights began to encircle him. A profound space law flitted upon his body as though it was dancing.

He brandished his ruler then slashed at the Ear Mice. With graceful ease, he had split the three smoke incarnations apart.

However, three more smoke incarnations instantly appeared not far away from him.

He took a slight step forward and seemed like he was about to charge towards them. But all of a sudden, he turned around and stabbed.

Puff! It sounded like something popped.

The Divine Farmer Ruler had pierced into the void. Then, blood started to fill the space where the Divine Farmer had stabbed.

At once, Tomos materialized and its body began to rapidly dissipate. It immediately turned into traces of green that gathered around the Divine Farmer Ruler.

"Do you think this pathetic little trick can deceive me?" the Divine Farmer asked with a cold and hard expression on his face.

Tomos' face didn't quite express any pain. In fact, it even revealed a sly smile. "Perhaps..."

As soon as it said this, its body quickly rotted and turned into a horriblelooking corpse. It seemed like this was still not its real body.

While watching this scene unfold before him, the Divine Farmer noticed a white and weightless bandage had materialized on the red crystal in his hand. The moment the bandage touched the red crystal, it had spread out and covered the red crystal in the blink of an eye.

The bandage had tightly wrapped itself around the red crystal. Suddenly, there was an awfully strong pulling force coming from the bandage.

Without any warning, it dragged the red crystal towards the sky.

The Divine Farmer was caught off guard by this abrupt move and the red crystal slipped out of his grasp.

However, he reacted very quickly. When he saw the red crystal being pulled away by the bandage, he instantly went after it and swiftly grabbed it in his hand.

But then, the Divine Farmer felt a powerful force pulling at the other end of the bandage. It was so strong that it also dragged him away. This force was utterly formidable.

"Well then, we will see who is stronger!"

As he said this, the Divine Farmer's face darkened. The power within his body suddenly erupted.

It was well-known that there was a huge gap between the Eternal Realm and the Holy Soul Realm warriors. They had huge differences in terms of physical strength, real strength, speed, and soul.

The moment the Divine Farmer's power had erupted, the bandage could no longer be pulled away from him. It couldn't budge for even a millimeter.

"Break!"

With a wave of the long ruler in his hand, he instantly severed the bandage off.

However, he frowned as he grasped the red crystal with his other hand. It didn't feel as heavy as it used to be. He felt a bad sense of foreboding.

He tore off the bandage in a hurry, only to find a big black stone inside it! "This can't be..."

The red crystal that contained Zen inside had actually been replaced! "My apologies."

Once again, Tomos appeared a short distance from the Divine Farmer. It bowed to him then turned into gray smoke and instantly dissipated.

The warriors at the Eternal Realm considered those at the Holy Soul Realm as weak beings.

Nevertheless, the number of warriors at the Holy Soul Realm in the Divine Farmer race was ten times bigger than that of the Black Ship.

The Divine Farmer thought that it didn't matter even if they had Other Shore Tokens from the Three Purities Stage. Their number was too small. It was not enough to fight against him because the gap in strength was just too huge.

But obviously, the members of the Black Ship were far stronger than the ordinary warriors at the Holy Soul Realm. With their cunning tricks and teamwork, they had actually managed to take away Zen from the Divine Farmer's hands! The Divine Farmer felt he was fooled. He had walked right into their trap.

This was extremely humiliating! He couldn't accept that he had fallen for their cheap tricks.

"How dare you play tricks on me? You will pay for this!"

The cultivated Divine Farmer finally showed a terrifyingly ferocious expression on his face.

A thin crack appeared on his forehead. It began to open slowly and revealed an eyeball. A triangular frame appeared on the surface of the eyeball.

Afterwards, there was a sudden flash of brilliant light.

After being punched by Fuxi, Usman had remained lying on the ground and gasping for breath. At this very moment, a triangular frame suddenly appeared in his eyes. At once, his body seemed like it was being controlled by his eyes. His eyeballs bulged and lifted his upper body with force. At the same time, his head spun in a strange angle.

Cracking sounds could be heard as his head spun around. Obviously, his neck was broken.

However, he didn't feel any pain. He closed his eyes and fell to the ground once more. He quickly had regained his consciousness.

When he woke up, he had no idea what had happened. But the severe pain from his neck made him wince and curse.

He looked around him and a strange and different sight was transmitted to the Divine Farmer's mind.

At that moment, he appeared as though he was looking down at the whole Separate Amber Province. He was able to see everything within the province very clearly. He continued to scan through the horizon. Soon enough, he noticed something a hundred miles away from him.

He saw a space ship floating alone in the void. The members of the Black Ship were either sitting or leaning inside it. The red crystal that contained Zen was dragged by a bandage into the space ship.

All these times, the Divine Farmer thought that his opponent must be the captain of the Black Ship.

He wouldn't be so angry if it was the captain of the Black Ship that was able to take Zen away. But now that he knew it was merely a group of warriors at the Holy Soul Realm who managed to easily abduct Zen, he was utterly infuriated.

"You will pay for this with your lives!"

All of a sudden, the Divine Farmer's figure became huge. With this, the Divine Farmer Ruler also grew in length and size.

He took a mere step forward and was able to cross a hundred miles. The Divine Farmer Ruler in his hand slashed towards the void.

With the slash, the void collapsed. The space ship couldn't remain intact.

Chapter 3853 Trapping Just then, several people joined hands to take away Zen's red crystal.

After Tomos stopped the crystal from being taken away with the smoke, he and Shera respectively used the illusion skill and the controlling technique to confuse Divine Farmer's judgment.

And indeed, Divine Farmer misjudged.

The 'bamboo pole' untied his bandage to wrap around the red crystal.

Meanwhile, another Black Ship member's skill was used to replace the red crystal with the stone.

It was the brass man who dragged the bandage, and he had a unique secret technique that allowed him to increase his strength threefold in a short period of time.

Once he activated the technique, the brass man was powerful enough to fight against even an Eternal Realm master.

In truth, if Divine Farmer was on full alert, even the Black Ship members could have a difficult time taking Zen away.

But Divine Farmer had always been on guard against the Black Ship's captain. Because he didn't quite take these people seriously, they found their chance to take action.

Now, in Divine Farmer's towering rage, he swung his ruler, slashing it down. The broken space spread all the way toward the space flying ship.

Inside, the members of the Black Ship had just brought in the red crystal, while Shera was leaning against the crystal to observe.

Just then, a crack in the sky rapidly spread over, shocking everyone with the sight.

"He found us out so soon." Tomo's eyes were full of astonishment.

"An Eternal Realm master naturally has the ability mysterious to anyone else. Edith, just transfer to another space." Shera turned around and gave the order.

In the corner of the space ship sat a blue-skinned woman with long locks.

Her Other Shore Token was passed to her by the Grandmaster of Heaven. It was the transparent flying ship docking in the void and happened to be the Invisible Ship in Stage Thirty-three of the Other Shore.

Theoretically, even an Eternal Realm master would find it difficult to find this ship—it wasn't one that could be easily sniffed out.

But the Black Ship people never expected Divine Farmer to make use of Usman's ability. Since the latter took control of the entire Separate Amber Province, everything there was in his view.

"Okay, Shera." Edith nodded.

She had a rather pitiful background—her very race had been exterminated, leaving solely her behind.

While she had never been particularly famous in the Black Ship, the other members of the Black Ship, Shera most especially, had always treated her very well.

In turn, Edith also treated Shera as her very own big sister.

With a flash of light in her gray eyes, the Invisible Ship suddenly collapsed, and the ruler of Divine Farmer then failed to hit it.

The entire space was concentrated at a single point. In the next moment, Edith had controlled the Invisible Ship, making it appear in another location a hundred miles away.

But the distance of a hundred miles was nothing to an Eternal Realm master.

Still, Edith and the rest of the Black Ship were highly confident in the Invisible Ship.

Divine Farmer couldn't discover it too soon, regardless.

But once Divine Farmer saw the ship disappear, his face grew dark as the eye in his forehead flashed again.

Usman was getting up from the ground.

The force of twisting his neck came from his own body just now, so this force was not transferred to the boundary wall.

In his confusion, he felt that his eyes bulged, dragging his entire head to twist.

"Again!"

This time, Usman was smarter about it.

So he merely jumped up and rotated his body along with the direction his eyeballs were circling in.

He had to turn in a full circle before his eyes recovered.

But the situation still left him just as clueless.

After finding the ship through Usman's eyes, Divine Farmer advanced again, slashing his ruler in the ship's direction.

The motion completely shocked Edith.

She was certain to leave no clue whatsoever when she moved the ship.

Even the Eternal Realm warriors couldn't track her. It was unimaginable that Divine Farmer was still able to do so.

"Keep moving!"

Before she could even finish calling out, the Invisible Ship disappeared once again.

But just as it moved, Divine Farmer managed to catch up, closing the distance between him and the ship.

At this point, the Black Ship people couldn't remain composed.

"How did he find us?"

"Look, he's coming again!"

"Was there any clue left on the red crystal?"

They searched frantically for a clue, completely reluctant to fight against Divine Farmer directly.

"Would Usman have told him how to find the ship?" Shera asked.

"It's possible..." Edith nodded, considering the thought.

Many years ago, Usman easily found the ship with a unique ability.

"That guy..." Even the brass man was deep in confusion, displeased.

While Usman had troubled the Black Ship before, never did it occur to them that Usman would dare do it again after being reborn—he was a natural troublemaker.

"What should we do? Should we find a way to kill Usman?" asked the "bamboo pole".

"We can't kill him. Even Fuxi can't kill him, let alone any of us," Shera said regretfully, shaking her head.

Seeing Divine Farmer approach, Edith had no time to even speak. The moment she reached a place, she had to move away immediately. If she was even a second slower, the Invisible Ship would be destroyed.

Usman suffered greatly under such a case.

Each time Divine Farmer checked the ship's location, Usman's eyes bulged and pulled him to a complete turn.

Yet if he didn't cooperate, his neck would be completely twisted off.

And so while people could see Usman constantly spinning in circles and cursing into the air, they had no clue what was happening to him.

Meanwhile, in the sky above the Separate Amber Province, the Black Ship's captain stood atop his ship's bow.

The edges of his black cloak were drenched in blood which seemed to be flowing somehow, heated up and emitting fine bubbles.

The ship's surface was also badly charred.

While there was no actual fire, the ship had been charred anyway, becoming suited to its name, Black Ship.

Before the captain was the huge shadow of Snake Goddess floating in the air. It had already stretched out its arms to envelop the entire ship, along with the captain.

And so the captain couldn't take action being directly confronted by the Snake Goddess.

"Snake Goddess, Divine Farmer has already attacked the Black Ship's members. With the strength of Divine Farmer, sooner or later, he'll be able to take Zen away. I don't think it's wise to fight me," the captain said.

It was Divine Farmer and the Black Ship members that fought over Zen, after all.

Regardless of who got the man, the result would be unacceptable to the Pear Hill.

"The Black Ship members may be only a group of Holy Soul Realm warriors, but they are not ordinary ones. Not long ago, it took only four of them to stop the Thunder Dimorphodon. No matter how powerful Divine Farmer is, the outcome will not be determined in such a short period of time." The Snake Goddess was shaking her head, highly confident in her own judgment.

"But what's the point of trapping me?" asked the captain again.

"It will be meaningful once Fuxi wins," responded the Snake Goddess calmly.

If Fuxi defeated Yellow Thearch, he'd have enough time and energy to fight for Zen. Whether or not there were other variables involved, she had to act accordingly.

In truth, at this point, the three forces were still testing each other—both the Snake Goddess and the captain were cautious, carefully trying to pick out each other's trump card.

Chapter 3854 Fuxi's Great Strength A small shadow soared through the air and crashed into the side of an enormous stone mountain, well over ten thousand feet in height. It had stood there, solid and immovable, for thousands of years. As soon as the shadow hit the stones, the mountain collapsed as though it had never existed.

Deep rumbling sounds echoed as the mountain crumbled from the force of the impact.

The huge mountain had been destroyed in the blink of an eye.

The stone shards of the mountain flew out in all directions. Many were sharp and deadly, and pierced through the nearby creatures like airborne weapons.

Most of the stabbed creatures died immediately. For all who lived in the mountain area, this day was the end of their world.

As the rumbles of the collapsing mountain began to fade, there was a strange buzzing noise.

A mark of the Eight Diagrams had appeared on the ruins of the mountain. A closer inspection revealed that the outer layer of the mark was blurry, because it was actually formed by the overlapping of many marks.

"Take this!"

A boom sounded.

For a moment, time seemed to stop and stand still.

Fuxi's arms were barely visible as he landed thousands of punches in very, very rapid succession. The speed and force of the punches released a great energy that flowed down from the ruins of the mountain.

But the buzzing sound continued.

The various noises merged with each other, each loud enough to obscure the original sounds, until only a continuous high-pitched note could be heard.

The overlapping marks of the Eight Diagrams exploded simultaneously.

The ground began to sink beneath the rubble of the mountain.

One thousand feet, ten thousand feet, one hundred thousand feet, one million feet...

The Source World was hollow, and almost all of its living beings lived in the inner layer. The outer layer was not thick. The thickest part was only sixty million feet at most, and the thinnest part was only a few million feet.

The majority of the exit points from the Source World were located in the weak spots of the outer layer.

The Separate Amber Province was itself located in a weak spot. The distance from its surface to the chaos outside was only more than ten million feet. Now, through sheer force, Fuxi had smashed it through.

In the chaos, the Yellow Thearch Sword exuded a golden light, ensuring the protection of the Yellow Thearch.

The golden light contained a holy way with the strongest defensive power.

However, even with such protection, the Yellow Thearch was still in a sorry state.

He had felt very confident since the defeat of the Nine Li race.

With the help of the Element Spirit race, his strength had improved by leaps and bounds. He became much more skillful in the use of his bloodline and the combination of Other Shore Tokens.

Meanwhile, Fuxi—who used to be honored as the strongest warrior at the Eternal Realm—was just an amateur. However, with his talent and fierce pursuit in the Three Purities Stage, he achieved what he had today.

Now, in the middle of the battle, the Yellow Thearch realized that he had underestimated Fuxi.

Fuxi didn't have many techniques. He didn't even rely on any Other Shore Token. He was simply strong.

Fuxi's relentless attack penetrated through the weak spot.

As he penetrated through the ground of Separate Amber Province, chaotic energy poured in through the hole, spreading throughout the province.

The energy burst into the Source World, emitting a buzzing noise.

The first wisp of chaotic energy swept past the rubble and came into contact with a blade of grass. In an instant, the green grass withered, blackened, and died.

For weaker creatures, chaotic energy was a deadly poison.

Many creatures in the vast Source World did not have the strength to resist the chaotic energy. Most of the aborigines in the Separate Amber Province would die.

"Your sword is very good. It saved your life," said Fuxi calmly, standing at the entrance of the hole.

Although he stood over one thousand feet away, his voice was clear and loud.

The Yellow Thearch floated in the chaos. He withdrew his sword and said grimly, "The sword is a part of me."

A lifeblood weapon was refined with one's own bloodline, so the Yellow Thearch's statement made sense.

"I knew the strength of your sword a long time ago," Fuxi replied. "If the Element Spirit race hadn't helped you to refine it, I would have broken it already." Fuxi spoke in a confident tone, as he stood in front of a hole he had punched through the very fabric of the Source World.

Especially now, he felt incomparably strong, as though there was nothing in the world that he couldn't break.

The Yellow Thearch slowly raised his sword above his head. "Everyone has their own lucky chances. I was lucky that I got the help of the Element Spirit race, and you were also lucky because you got the secret blood inheritance."

As he talked, the Yellow Thearch Sword emitted a golden light, and three holy ways appeared. They were one of his most powerful theurgies.

"But luck isn't the most important factor! In the end, strength and weakness matter the most," said the Yellow Thearch. With a gentle motion, he shook his long sword.

The three holy ways intertwined and headed straight for Fuxi in the Separate Amber Province.

"Today you will learn what real strength is!"

Fuxi said coldly. He did not try to evade the attack. He stood directly in its path and raised his fist as he saw the three holy ways rushing towards him.

He didn't care what kind of theurgy the Yellow Thearch used. He was certain that whatever attack came his way, he would be able to block it and smash it into pieces.

The holy ways swooped towards him.

Several marks of the Eight Diagrams appeared on the holy ways. Fuxi threw several punches, and the marks immediately exploded.

But the holy ways were not broken by the explosion. They seemed like illusions, impervious to the impact of Fuxi's blows.

The holy ways seemed to be both concrete and ethereal, and they behaved in an unpredictable manner.

"Fists are not enough for the holy ways," the Yellow Thearch said with a sneer. "Now let's see if you have any real strength."

The three illusory holy ways surrounded Fuxi, and cracks began to form in the golden light. Soon, the holy ways reformed into a thin net that enclosed Fuxi.

The Yellow Thearch left his spot.

In an instant, he appeared outside the net. He gazed at Fuxi, trapped within the crisscrossing lines.

The golden light emanated continuously from the surface of the Yellow Thearch Sword. He thrust the sword forward, and a terrifying energy was released from the thin strands of the net. Every line turned into sharp golden sword radiance, shrinking towards Fuxi in the center of the net.

"Shatter!" commanded the Yellow Thearch.

Instantly, it was as though thousands of swords slashed at Fuxi.

The Yellow Thearch launched this attack with all his strength.

He was so focused that his very bloodline seemed to boil, and his eyes glowed with a golden light. He put all his energy into attacking Fuxi, wanting to tear him to pieces.

The golden sword radiance slashed into Fuxi's body.

The net had shrunk and now completely enveloped Fuxi until he was no longer visible.

In that moment, the sword radiance exploded, and it was so bright that even the sun looked dim in comparison.

In the far distance, the powerful warriors of the Oneness Sky Palace, the Bearing race and the Divine Farmer race paused briefly amid their fighting to glance at the golden glow of sword radiance on the horizon.

However, the Yellow Thearch was not Emperor Charm. The swordsmanship he cultivated was completely different from Emperor Charm's Nine-Sun World Destruction Theurgy.

Several moments passed before the golden light dissipated completely.

Something unexpected had happened. When the Yellow Thearch saw the result of his attack, his eyes widened, and one eyelid began twitching with alarm.

Fuxi stood there, entirely unharmed. He wore a slight, sardonic smile as he said, "Well, you said my fists are weak, but your sword seems even weaker! You have no true strength! You are weak."

Fuxi's eyes glinted as he repeated, "Weak!"

With that final word, Fuxi vanished.

The marks of the Eight Diagrams appeared and rushed towards the Yellow Thearch.

Fuxi came into view, threw a punch, and disappeared again.

The Yellow Thearch couldn't follow Fuxi's motions because he was moving at an unimaginable speed. Every time he caught a glimpse of Fuxi, he was in a different position. This made it difficult, if not impossible, for the Yellow Thearch to launch a counterattack.

This put the Yellow Thearch at a severe disadvantage. He was forced to passively wait to see what Fuxi planned to do, without any chance to fight back.

Chapter 3855 The Land Of Ancient Flesh The huge shadow of Snake Goddess stayed still up in the sky as its arms held the black ship.

Snake Goddess and the captain of the Black Ship previously used their own methods to learn about the full situation, and they also watched the battle between Fuxi and the Yellow Thearch.

Just now, the captain of the Black Ship thought that the Snake Goddess was too confident. After all, the Yellow Thearch was still quite powerful, and it wasn't easy for Fuxi to take him down.

When they fought, however, it was evident that they were far too different.

Fuxi was much more powerful than everyone had expected. The captain quickly grew serious, and he said, "It seems that there is a reason for your confidence in the Human Sovereign."

"Of course," the Snake Goddess said with a glint in her cat-like eyes.

"But, are you confident enough to trap me here?" At that moment, the captain looked at the shadow of Snake Goddess above his head.

If Fuxi had really killed the Yellow Thearch, then the members of the Black Ship and the Divine Farmer would fall into Fuxi's hands no matter who won.

The mere thought of it made the captain restless.

"If you want to try, you can do it with Mahoney," the Snake Goddess calmly said as she looked towards the void on the left.

The area exhibited a wave of space fluctuation, and Mahoney, who was hiding inside, appeared.

"You are quite keen, Snake Goddess," she said.

"Your whispers are too loud," the Snake Goddess replied.

At first, Mahoney planned to attack the captain, but the captain asked his crew to fight, so things changed.

She had been hiding in the dark and waiting for a good chance. She never thought that the Yellow Thearch would be disadvantaged, so she took the initiative to communicate with the captain.

While all of that happened, the Snake Goddess had cleverly captured the wave of their consciousness. "I wonder who is stronger, you or the Human Sovereign?" the captain asked.

In reality, Fuxi's power scared the captain. He hadn't seen the Snake Goddess fight for a long time. If she was as strong as Fuxi, then things would get tricky.

The captain was first quite confident in himself. He thought that he was as strong as the Yellow Thearch, so when he saw that the Yellow Thearch got defeated all the time, he became not that confident.

Confidence was the foundation of strength, but arrogance that grew out of confidence was a hindrance to survival.

The captain had what he had today because he never underestimated any of his opponents.

The Snake Goddess looked down and shook her head. "If I were the Human Sovereign, and the Yellow Thearch didn't have another trump card, he would have died," she commented.

Upon hearing those words, Mahoney and the captain frowned.

Did the Snake Goddess mean that she was stronger than Fuxi? "If so, then we can only try," the captain stated.

A cyan Other Shore Token appeared on the surface of Mahoney's body. It was the Spearhead Armor of Destruction that Emperor Charm had worn.

Then, a powerful force continuously gathered within her body.

The Snake Goddess gently raised her head and put her hands on either side.

Her large shadow followed suit and waved its hands to slap both the captain's and Mahoney's heads.

Swish! The shadow of Snake Goddess was made out of pure energy and could erode almost anything.

Furthermore, it was much purer than those of the people of Pear Hill because she was their leader.

In turn, Mahoney flew backward to avoid the energy beams.

Meanwhile, the captain of the Black Ship stood at the side and waited for the shadow of Snake Goddess to descend from the sky. As soon as her shadow landed on the black ship, his black cloak exploded.

A bald man emerged from the black cloak. He was covered in a thin layer of scales and had two sharp horns on his forehead.

The captain didn't resist but let the energy beam hit him.

Crack! Crack! Crack! Some of the long and thin energy beams at the end of the shadow of Snake Goddess landed on the black ship.

The black ship immediately shattered, while the energy eroded its wooden body and set it on fire.

Then, the energy beams in the middle lashed at the captain's skin and burned him. Bright red blood gushed out of his charred black scars.

The Snake Goddess found it strange that the captain didn't dodge. However, she would never hesitate in such a battle.

Since he didn't avoid the attacks, she would kill him first.

The fabric of her golden dress fluttered when she slightly twisted her waist.

Her shadow followed her and turned around, then forced Mahoney back with ease.

Afterwards, she reached out her other hand towards the captain.

Her shadow also did the same thing with one hand and the tentacle-like energy beams wrapped around the captain.

The erosion caused by the pure energy beams was terrible, especially since they came from the shadow of Snake Goddess.

The energy beams went into the captain's body at a visible speed. Blood spurted out of his sunken body, then the energy beams quickly evaporated it.

Mahoney was stunned when she saw the scene.

Was the captain trying to get himself killed? Would the Snake Goddess kill him in that way? Or perhaps the Snake Goddess had used a method that made the captain unable to dodge? Multiple thoughts swam in Mahoney's head. She now wanted to escape as quickly as possible.

On the other hand, the energy beams quickly eroded the captain's body into two. His whole body melted like a candle. He would surely die.

Still, the Snake Goddess didn't feel relaxed at all. She didn't think that the captain was dead. Instead, she remained highly vigilant and stared straight at the other black ships not far away.

"The power of your shadow is truly extraordinary." The captain's voice floated over. This time, he appeared on another black ship.

"What?"

Just then, Mahoney squinted to get a closer look.

Truth was, it wasn't difficult to get a physical avatar with their strength. It also wasn't hard to distinguish if the opponent was a real body or an avatar.

Mahoney just saw that the shadow of Snake Goddess had eroded the captain's real body. How did he reappear? Maybe he had used some rare Other Shore Token to bring himself back to life, but there was no reason for him to let the Snake Goddess kill him once.

"It seems that the rumor is true," said the Snake Goddess. She bit her lips, crossed her hands, and waved them.

"I heard that the captain of the Black Ship doesn't have a real body. These ships are your bodies!"

Whoosh! Whoosh! Whoosh! The moment she finished speaking, countless energy beams lashed towards the black ships like whips.

Most people thought that the Black Ship was an intimidating force, but the real strong ones were its members. The ships were just ordinary flying ships.

Without the help of those at the Eternal Realm, the ordinary warriors at the Holy Soul Realm or even the Chaotic Source Realm could destroy them.

But when the Snake Goddess's energy beams struck the ships, there was only a muffled sound, and the beams just bounced off the ships' surfaces.

The powerful energy beams had lost their desired effect. "In addition to the fact that my real bodies are the ships, I wonder what else you have found out?" the captain said from the ship.

The Snake Goddess thought for a while before she asked hesitantly, "Have you integrated with the Land of Ancient Flesh?" The Land of Ancient Flesh was an immensely dangerous place.

It was quite a small land in the far south of the Three Purities Stage, but it was frightening and forbidden.

After all, its exterior was a large piece of flesh.

It also had a distinct feature. Any power could only work there once. The second and succeeding times, they would be ineffective.

Chapter 3856 In The Black Ship The Land of Ancient Flesh was a whole large chunk of flesh located in the far south of the Three Purities Stage.

Though no one knew who explored the Land of Ancient Flesh first, it could be assumed that it was easy to break into the place in the beginning.

However, after someone dug into the land once, no pure physical force could work on it anymore. Because of this, the very first mark on the ground could still be seen to this very day.

After one used fire to melt the Land of Ancient Flesh, they found that it would only successfully melt off a small piece. Since then, the Land of Ancient Flesh grew immune to the fire, and no longer feared any flames.

All of these failed attempts led to the conclusion that methods and attempts only worked once when used on the Land of Ancient Flesh.

This large chunk of flesh seemed to have developed this rare evolutionary ability, which worked very well to its advantage.

At this point, the Land of Ancient Flesh had endured so many attacks that it was basically unstoppable. The flesh feared nothing now.

Many people had attempted to break it, including the Snake Goddess and Fuxi and others. However, they failed to cause even a dent in the Land of Ancient Flesh.

Just now, the Snake Goddess used her shadow and corroded the body of the Black Ship's captain. The captain didn't dodge because he wanted to adapt to the energy beams from the shadow of Snake Goddess.

After the captain experienced the power of the beams, the shadow of Snake Goddess became an ineffective attack to the black ships.

It was in this moment that the Snake Goddess realized that this resistance possibly had something to do with the Land of Ancient Flesh.

Because of the flesh's extraordinary characteristic, many people attempted to obtain the land to use its powers. However, it was due to this evolutionary characteristic alone that no one succeeded.

In theory, the Land of Ancient Flesh could not be sliced, separated, much less be merged with anyone. If this was so, how did the captain of the Black Ship merge himself with such an incredible Other Shore Token? "You are quite smart to have understood it so quickly," the captain smirked, "Please do aboard the ship and stay there for a while."

As soon as the captain finished speaking, the black ship closest in proximity to the Snake Goddess suddenly swooped down in her direction.

Just then, Snake Goddess tapped her toes in the air and flew backward rapidly, her long dress flowing gracefully in the air along with her.

Normally, the Snake Goddess's speed should have been enough for her to escape, but the black ship suddenly produced a space fluctuation. Within a second, the Snake Goddess noticed the light dimmed around her, and she was already within the black ship.

It was a gloomy, quiet cabin and no matter how much the ship sped up, jolted or swayed, the people inside it were stable and unbothered.

"Buzz!"

In an attempt to leave, the Snake Goddess tried to use the Grand Teleportation and exit.

However, as soon as the space channel appeared and opened up, it vanished just as quickly.

It was obvious that the captain of the Black Ship already had used the power of space to contain her earlier. Because the ship had evolved, the power of space was unusable inside it.

"Buzz, buzz, buzz..."

Just then, the swords that hung on the wooden wall behind the Snake Goddess shook and vibrated. Suddenly, they shot up and pointed straight at her.

"Whoosh, whoosh, whoosh, whoosh..."

It was as if a hidden person controlled the short swords and aimed towards the Snake Goddess. Though the swords were short, they had immense power within them.

The Snake Goddess's body dodged and avoided the short swords. However, the nearby mast against the wall spun three hundred and sixty degrees and fell towards her.

Caught off guard, all the Snake Goddess could do was raise her arms to block it.

With a loud bang, she was sent right into a wall. When her body collided with the wall, numerous spears hovered at the end of the passageway, ready to shoot her.

It seemed that everything in the black ship was a part of the captain - and they were all more or less fatal.

Initially, Mahoney stood by and watched the fight from a distance.

However, when she saw that the Snake Goddess was devoured by the black ship, a feeling of apprehension slowly consumed her.

She had originally discussed with the captain of the Black Ship that they were going to join forces to deal with the Snake Goddess. As of the moment, this didn't seem like the case.

It suddenly occurred to her that she and the captain were on opposing sides.

A strong sense of urgency rose within her, but just as she was about to use the Grand Teleportation, a black ship swooped down and engulfed her within a few seconds.

Once the two warriors of the Eternal Realm were trapped, a third black ship descended towards Divine Farmer this time.

Since Fuxi and Yellow Thearch were still at war against one another, the captain figured that if he trapped the Divine Farmer, he could easily take Zen away.

For the captain, his plan was fool proof. This was going to be too easy.

Meanwhile, Divine Farmer chased after the Invisible Ship with the Divine Farmer Ruler gripped in his hand.

At the same time, Edith concentrated on controlling the Invisible Ship to dodge Divine Farmer, but to no avail. Anywhere she went, Divine Farmer appeared right after.

"Buzz!"

A few moments later, both the Invisible Ship and Divine Farmer appeared in the north corner of the Separate Amber Province.

Edith didn't have enough time to control the ship to dodge this time.

"Ghoul Substitute!"

Shera stretched out her arms and gripped hard, as if she held onto thin, invisible threads. All of a sudden, a huge monster that was made up of corpses hovered right above the Invisible Ship.

The ghoul had cost Shera years to piece together, so it possessed extremely strong defensive power.

However, no matter how powerful a ghoul was, it would never be able to resist a single blow from Divine Farmer.

"Puff!"

Just like that, the huge ghoul was sliced in half by the ruler, and it spewed green blood left and right.

As Shera saw her ghoul get killed in one strike, her eyes filled up with sadness. However, this did not mean the efforts were useless. Because the ghoul blocked the ruler, it gave Edith the window to teleport away.

"We can't go on like this. How about I go out and stop him? Edith, you must take everyone away," the brass man spoke out.

The people of the Black Ship were not naturally a united group in normal times. After all, they had already been tainted as evil in the Source World, and each one of them had done repulsive things in the past.

However, when it came to sacrifice and saving their members, they didn't hesitate at all.

After they lived on the Black Ship for so long, they eventually became a part of it.

"You can't stop him all by yourself," Shera snapped back.

"No, but at least I can buy you some time." Just then, the surface of the brass man's body turned yellow and solid like an iron wall. Without asking for any help, he prepared to sacrifice himself.

"Let's attack together. Let Edith take the red crystal to leave first," another creature spoke from not too far away. He was Vance, half human and half deer and a longtime member of the Black Ship.

"I agree." Shera nodded. "Even if we fight head on, we won't necessarily lose."

If the members of the Black Ship teamed up, they would have enough strength to put up against a warrior at the Eternal Realm. After all, it was not long ago that the Black Ship trapped the Thunder Dimorphodon with only four of them.

However, the strength of warriors at the Eternal Realm also varied in amount and energy. A warrior like Divine Farmer was obviously among the more powerful ones at the Eternal Realm. No one on the Black Ship was willing to face such a powerful existence unless it was an utmost necessity.

Left with absolutely no choice, they decided to fight Divine Farmer head-on and as a team.

All of a sudden, the Invisible Ship moved through spatial transference again.

As usual, Divine Farmer appeared behind it like a taunting shadow. Once he slashed down with the ruler, the brass man was already out of the Invisible Ship.

A light emerged from the brass man's body, and just like that, the aura of an Other Shore Token surged out from him.

At the same time, a huge brass pillar appeared in his right hand as he charged towards the sky! "Crack!"

With one attempt, the strike of Divine Farmer's ruler hit the brass pillar precisely. The brass pillar cracked right at the middle, and as if it was made out of soft mud, the crack trickled down all the way to the bottom of the pillar.

The Combat Dragon Pillar, which was the brass man's prized weapon, was destroyed in an instant.

Chapter 3857 Combat Dragon Absorb After Divine Farmer had destroyed the Combat Dragon Pillar with the ruler, he slashed at the brass man once more.

Just as his second strike was about to land on the brass man, a bandage suddenly wrapped around his arm.

At the other end of the bandage was the "bamboo pole".

The "bamboo pole" glowed with colorful light after the bandage unwrapped. In the Black Ship, the "bamboo pole" was the most proficient in using poison. Back then, when the first Usman appeared, he also relied on his fast-spreading "Flash Insect Poison" to make thousands of the provinces in the Source World turn red.

Whoosh! The "bamboo pole" then pulled the bandage and passed by the brass man and rushed towards Divine Farmer.

His whole body shone brightly and had turned into a semi-liquid state.

Under his skin was not flesh, but water.

"Whoosh!"

Meanwhile, the ruler slashed down and sank into the body of the "bamboo pole." In turn, the "bamboo pole" immediately softened and turned into a mass of sticky venom that spread out on Divine Farmer's arms! "Sizzle..."

As soon as the venom came into contact with Divine Farmer, his arms became pitch black. The black spread at an alarming speed, and in no time, it reached his forearms.

"You used poison on me? How naive of you!"

The Divine Farmer Ruler he held emitted a green light that rolled towards him. The light mildly surrounded his arms and turned them back to normal.

Then, the remaining green light followed the spreading venom.

In reality, the venom was the real body of the "bamboo pole". It was his trump card. It liquefied his form and turned it into a toxic liquid that he used to attack.

Although the "bamboo pole" hadn't reached the Eternal Realm, he was a much-experienced warrior in the Black Ship. He was ranked third on the Black Ship in terms of age.

He had liquefied himself into poison three times in the past. It took him a long time to recover every time he was liquefied, and the recovery process was painful. However, he was always successful in killing opponents who were very difficult to deal with, including a warrior at the Eternal Realm.

This time, however, his opponent was Divine Farmer! Furthermore, the ball of green light Divine Farmer used was fatal to him.

He immediately felt chills when he saw the green light. He wanted to escape, but it was too late. The green light had already entangled with the venom, then the venom neutralized and disappeared.

"Bane!"

"Damn it!"

When the real body of the "bamboo pole" got destroyed, two more warriors charged towards Divine Farmer from both sides.

The person on the left carried a huge saber, and his name was Alonzo, and the person on the right was Shera.

The two of them had a good relationship with the "bamboo pole", whose name was Bane. There was no way they weren't going to do anything when the green light from the Divine Farmer Ruler melted him! "Buzz!"

At that moment, a strange dark mark appeared on the surface of the great saber on Alonzo's back. Then, he lifted the saber and swung it at Divine Farmer's head.

The black saber radiance cut towards Divine Farmer with an irresistible and overpowering force.

Aside from the captain, the strongest one among the thirteen members of the Black Ship was probably Alonzo.

Unfortunately, the Eternal Realm was far too stronger than the Holy Soul Realm, especially when the warrior of the Eternal Realm was Divine Farmer, who had a powerful lifeblood weapon.

Alonzo's strike, which seemed to be able to chop the heaven and earth, only made a muffled sound when it touched the Divine Farmer Ruler. The black saber radiance disappeared. The strange mark on the great saber disintegrated, and so did the whole saber itself.

"Phew!"

After Divine Farmer blocked the attack, he slapped Alonzo with his ruler.

Bang! The strike landed squarely on Alonzo's head. Although he had Chaotic Source Spirits to protect him, even a single strike from a warrior like Divine Farmer contained over one hundred thousand divine megatons of force.

Thus, Alonzo's Chaotic Source Spirits quickly became exhausted, and at the same time, his head turned into a mass of blood.

Then, he turned into a headless corpse and fell.

"Alonzo!"

Shera's eyes turned dark red as she stretched out her hand and tried to grab Divine Farmer's head.

On the other and, Divine Farmer didn't even look at her. Instead, he raised his ruler.

"Da!"

However, Shera had grabbed the Divine Farmer Ruler! Divine Farmer didn't expect that the woman who reeked of corpses could resist his strike. In turn, he immediately tried to pull the ruler out of her hand.

Even then, Shera's white jade-like hand still tightly held on to the ruler like a pincer.

Divine Farmer was utterly shocked. "How could your hand have such power?" he asked in disbelief.

Ordinary people didn't smell Shera's stench. Or, maybe she didn't stink like that at first, but because she was always around the dead, she eventually smelled like them.

She was a mere cultivator at the Holy Soul Realm who strengthened her body to the point that she could fight a warrior in the Eternal Realm. It was indeed something that surprised Divine Farmer.

Just as Shera had bought more time, three more members of the Black Ship came over.

Of course, they wouldn't let such a fleeting opportunity pass by.

Then again, they were far too different when it came to strength. Moreover, the remaining members became chaotic and couldn't cooperate well anymore due to the deaths of Bane and Alonzo.

While that happened, Divine Farmer tapped Shera's head with his other hand to force her to retreat.

As Shera retreated, Divine Farmer had already pulled out the ruler, and the ruler whirled around his back.

Puff! Puff! Puff! One of the three members of the Black Ship was cut into two at the waist, and the other two lost their arms.

Although they wouldn't die, they couldn't fight in a short time.

"Whoosh!"

When Divine Farmer had taken down several members of the Black Ship in a row, he flew towards the Invisible Ship.

Inside the Invisible Ship was Edith, who was visibly anxious. No matter where she went, the Divine Farmer followed closely behind. What made it worse was that the other members of the Black Ship couldn't defeat him.

When panic was about to overtake her, the brass man appeared in the Invisible Ship again.

"What are you doing?" she asked. She didn't know why the brass man returned.

The brass man did not answer and only stared fiercely at Zen's red crystal.

Then, he stretched both of his hands and put it on his shoulder.

"Combat Dragon Absorb!"

He roared, then his hands released a faint mist and fused him with the red crystal.

It turned out that the Combat Dragon Pillar that Divine Farmer had just broken was not an Other Shore Token, but a weapon that the captain of the Black Ship had made for him.

The brass man's Other Shore Token could combine his weapon and his body into one. He had always used the Combat Dragon Pillar to fight, and now Divine Farmer had destroyed it. Of course, it was hard to find a suitable weapon in a short time. Suddenly, he thought of the red crystal. So he placed it on his shoulder and merged it with his body.

Right after that, he left the Invisible Ship and rushed towards Divine Farmer! Now, the reason Divine Farmer had chased the Invisible Ship for so long was because of Zen.

The second he saw the brass man rush towards him, his face became unreadable.

The red crystal was undoubtedly a good material to use, but wouldn't that be giving him what he wanted by using Zen as a weapon and coming to him? Therefore, he didn't dodge and instead charged forward as well.

Once again, he used the Divine Farmer Ruler to slash through the air and swung it at the red crystal! "Bang!"

"Crack!"

The first strike failed to shatter the red crystal, but the second strike finally broke it.

"Combat Dragon Absorb!"

White mist burst out from the brass man's hands.

Since the red crystal was damaged, he could no longer use it as a weapon.

Thus, he made up his mind. He took Zen's body inside the red crystal and merged with it.

Chapter 3858 A Good Weapon There was no way the brass man could think of anything else during this critical moment.

He knew that Zen was the crux of all these matters and was the reason for Divine Farmer's chase.

They wanted Zen for a specific purpose and until this purpose was fulfilled, there was no way they would harm him.

It was fortunate that the brass man's conjecture turned out to be true. Divine Farmer's frown was very obvious when he decided to use Zen as a weapon.

Divine Farmer, Yellow Thearch, and Mahoney all received the same order from the Element Spirit race: take advantage of Zen's inability to leave the Other Shore and capture him! Seeing the brass man carry Zen on his shoulders as he rushed towards him, Divine Farmer had no choice but to tilt his Divine Farmer Ruler to hit the brass man's head and avoid harming Zen.

Given his rich experience in combat, the brass man easily saw through his opponent's move. He ducked and swung Zen's body forward to use him as a shield! Determined to protect himself, the brass man raised Zen's body and smashed it towards the Divine Farmer.

In fear of hurting Zen, Divine Farmer chose to withdraw his ruler. In his haste, he did not have enough time to dodge the swipe heading towards him and could only take the force of the attack head-on! Bang! Zen's head directly slammed onto Divine Farmer's chest with a loud thud.

The impact was so strong and penetrated deep into Divine Farmer's chest, through his heart, and onto his spine.

This strong, penetrating force was the result of the brass man's theurgy: the Combat Dragon Power.

It did not just stop with the Divine Farmer's body, in fact, the same power erupted on several thousand feet of ground behind him. The amount of destruction caused by this theurgy was terrifying and could very well play a decisive effect in normal combat.

Divine Farmer's body trembled and the sharp pain he felt in his chest confirmed his injuries.

A murderous glint flashed through his eyes, furious that this brass man managed to deal such heavy damage to him. Divine Farmer quickly made a dash and came upon his opponent's back.

He raised his Divine Farmer Ruler and brought it down! Clatter! The surface of his weapon glowed an ominous dark green as numerous black carvings flowed through it.

Divine Farmer was good at detoxification but he was also considered an expert at weaponizing poison.

This Willow Green Poison, for example, was a unique concoction Divine Farmer himself created.

It was so potent that not even an Eternal Realm master could hope to survive it.

He did not normally use this on Holy Soul Realm opponents but the rage he felt from being hoodwinked by the brass man was enough to make him pull out all his cards.

Unfortunately for him, the brass man was also set to go all out in this fight.

Although Divine Farmer's agility was on par with his, all the brass man really needed to do was be fast enough to wield Zen as his shield.

As the poisonous ruler headed towards him, the brass man quickly brandished Zen as his primary defense. He didn't even need to turn around.

This counterattack was so sudden that Divine Farmer couldn't react in time.

He watched in horror as his Divine Farmer Ruler chopped down towards Zen's body and he was unable to stop it.

Bang! There was a loud, clanging sound as the weapon hit Zen's leg. Instead of going through the flesh, it was as if another weapon collided with the ruler.

The sound and sight shocked not only Divine Farmer and the brass man but the rest of the Black Ship's members.

There was no way the brass man expected Divine Farmer to hit Zen so carelessly.

Meanwhile, Divine Farmer was at his wits' end in fear of Zen dying from his poison.

However, what astonished everyone was that Zen remained unharmed through this entire ordeal.

The attack dealt by Divine Farmer had at least one hundred thousand divine megatons of force! How in the world was Zen able to resist such a blow? Could it be that his Chaotic Source Spirits managed to absorb the attack and saved his life? Were his Chaotic Source Spirits truly so strong that they were able to resist one hundred thousand divine megatons of force? The exchange of blows boosted the brass man's confidence. It was basically a confirmation that he could choose to wield Zen as an invincible weapon, so he carried the man towards Divine Farmer. "Brothers of the Black Ship! Lend me a hand!"

Ready to answer his call, a member of the Black Ship stretched out his hand and patted the top of his skull where an Other Shore Token emerged. It was a black and withered branch.

"Withering Power!"

This was similar to the Latent Theurgy Zen once used to resist Elizabeth in the past! Another member of the Black Ship patted his chest and a small circular lens appeared. He quickly chucked it towards the brass man.

"Power Transfer Lens!"

Buzz! These two Other Shore Tokens worked well together: the Withering Power released by the black withered branch, that could increase one's strength sixfold, was reflected by the lens. The brass man could easily feel its effects rush through him.

Since the brass man was a power type warrior, his full strength could very well reach over fifty thousand divine megatons! Such formidable strength truly stood out among all Holy Soul Realm warriors and could easily reach the threshold of the Eternal Realm! However, with the use of Withering Power, his strength soared to three hundred thousand divine megatons! So long as these two other members of the Black Ship continued to assist him then the brass man could continuously unleash such frightening amounts of power.

Whoosh! Whoosh! Whoosh! A white mist began to emanate from the brass man's hand that held Zen's body. He felt really good considering the significant increase in his strength.

Though cooperation wasn't a strange concept to the Black Ship, this was the first time they used such a strategy against such a powerful being like Divine Farmer.

"Go to hell!"

Whoosh! Even Divine Farmer faltered in the face of this ferocious attack.

He fully intended to avoid this all-powerful force headed his way but he was also worried and wondered if Zen would be able to withstand the brass man's super-strength.

Before Divine Farmer could come up with a decision, another Black Ship member decided to intervene. It was Edith, the controller of the Invisible Ship.

"Invisible Ship!" she commanded.

The Invisible Ship itself was an Other Shore Token. Although it was virtually useless in combat, it had other functions that could be put to good use.

"Space Imprisonment!" In times of need, the Invisible Ship could be used as an escape method or a way to trap enemies.

With Edith's command, the Invisible Ship instantly disassembled into countless, transparent space fragments that recombined into a space cage intended to trap Divine Farmer.

Given Divine Farmer's strength, it wouldn't be that difficult for him to break out of this space cage if he had the time, around twelve seconds to be exact.

However, when Edith trapped him inside, she also let the brass man in! Divine Farmer was essentially cornered! There was nowhere left he could run to escape the brass man's attack! A wicked grin flashed through his opponent's face. "Divine Farmer! Let's see if you can withstand this!" he shouted.

The brass man could feel the blood within his body boil as his mist-covered hands raised Zen's body and smashed it against Divine Farmer's head.

Left with no other choice, Divine Farmer slid his fingers across the Divine Farmer Ruler.

Buzz...
