Green light flashed from the ruler and spread all throughout his body, like a blossoming willow.

Just as the light began to shine, Zen's head made contact with Divine Farmer's body.

Pop! Despite the harsh blow, Divine Farmer was unharmed.

However, his once indestructible Divine Farmer Ruler twisted so suddenly.

Pop! Determined to not give Divine Farmer any chance to recover, the brass man quickly smashed Zen down on him.

This second attack twisted the Divine Farmer Ruler even more and completely distorted its shape.

Pop! Upon the third smash, Divine Farmer fell back and smashed the space cage Edith trapped him in.

His weapon was now greatly distorted but at least he managed to withstand three, incredibly fatal attacks! Of course, the state of his Divine Farmer Ruler made his heart ache. It would take a long time to nurture his lifeblood weapon back into shape.

Still, Zen's unharmed state concerned him more. How in the world was the young man completely intact after enduring intense bouts of power? A look of regret flashed through the brass man's face when he realized that he had failed to subdue Divine Farmer. Just a few more smashes and he was certain to have ended him. It would take the brass man a few seconds to realize that the astonishment on Divine Farmer's face wasn't directed at him, but to Zen whom he wielded as a weapon.

'Well, I got to admit this boy's physical body makes for a good weapon, ' the brass man thought to himself.

Then he remembered that Zen withstood nearly three hundred thousand divine megatons of force but was barely injured.

It wasn't long before the brass man's face was the exact mirror of astonishment on Divine Farmer's.

Chapter 3859 The Growing Light Column In the far northwest of the Source World, there was a unique copper tree.

The roots of the tree reached deep into the ground. After growing for a long time, it was now able to extract a very special type of copper ore from the deep underground and absorb the ore into its core.

This copper was very flexible, and its raw form, which was viscous liquid, gave it the name "water copper".

The water copper could be cut with a knife easily.

But once a huge force came into contact with it, it would automatically become solid and extremely hard in an instant. All in all, instead of a type of ore, it could also be described as a kind of liquid with magical properties.

Based on these properties, the captain of the Black Ship finally built the Combat Dragon Pillar for the brass man.

The brass man had wanted to test the effect of the Combat Dragon Pillar before, so he used the Power Transfer Lens and the Withering Power to exert a force of nearly three hundred thousand divine megatons on the pillar. The result was satisfying for him—the pillar could take on the force easily.

Therefore, the stronger the force the Combat Dragon Pillar received, the stronger it'd become.

Had the brass man possessed three hundred thousand divine megatons of force before, Divine Farmer wouldn't have been able to cut the Combat Dragon Pillar.

But at that time, the brass man had only relied on his own strength when he used the Combat Dragon Absorb, so the Combat Dragon Pillar was naturally destroyed by Divine Farmer with a casual strike of his ruler.

Now, however, the brass man's weapon wasn't the "Combat Dragon Pillar"—his weapon now was a human's body.

Although Zen was basically an Eternal Realm warrior, a force of three hundred thousand divine megatons wasn't a laughing matter. Even a warrior like Zen would still have his body crushed if his body was struck by such a force! Everything the brass man did just now was done on the spur of the moment and without any further consideration at all. Now that he calmed down, he realized that what happened didn't at all make any sense.

On Zen's Three Purities Stone in the Grand Plain Stage, Zen's anchor bodies changed.

The force exerted on Zen's real physical body had been transmitted to his anchor bodies.

One's anchor body was connected to the Eternal Scroll Painting, and the Eternal Scroll Painting was connected to the Eternal Divine Courtyard.

When the force was transmitted to Zen's anchor bodies, an imperceptible wave of energy was also transmitted to the sacred cup in the Eternal Divine Courtyard at an unimaginable speed.

Pa! Zen's body shook. Consequently, even the entire sacred cup shook.

After the tiny ripples on the surface of the thick blood in the cup died out, the map in the circle of light on the ground began to change.

There were originally two light columns rising in the map. Each of them respectively represented the bloodline of Chiyou and the bloodline of the Chaos Ancient God. These two light columns both had a life attribute, so they were in the lower left area.

However, after Zen took on the three hundred thousand divine megatons of force, another light column grew several inches tall in the fan-shaped area on the lower right side, the area which represented destruction! Complicated expressions appeared on the faces of the four bronze statues on the square.

It was already hard to believe that this guy was able to perform the Blood Merge Reconstruction.

Now, he also wasn't playing by the rules? Generally, even if a qualified person succeeded in obtaining the recognition of the ancestry-level bloodline, the shape of the map would be set in the shortest amount of time and wouldn't change again.

Zen had been lying motionless in the sacred cup for a long time, so why did the light column in the map grow again? This looked like he was cheating.

However, as long as there was a light column connected to the edge of the circle of light, it meant that he was acknowledged by the ancestry-level bloodline and also obtained the ancestry-level bloodline.

There were 373 light columns in total. How great the potential of the ancestry-level bloodline one merged with was would depend on how much potential the warriors in the sacred cup had and how many light columns they connected.

"Something seems wrong with the ancestry-level bloodline, don't you think?"

"If this light column can also reach the circle of light, then this kid will have three light columns connected to the circle of light..."

"The best record in the Eternal Divine Courtyard is fourteen light columns.

It happened a very long time ago, and unlike what he's doing now. The warrior, who made that record, made the fourteen light columns grow in one go…"

The four bronze statues were all staring at Zen. A faint trace of excitement was apparent in their eyes.

Their sense of duty made them wish that everything would go as usual, so when Zen first appeared, they were quite hostile to him.

At this moment, however, their thoughts had somewhat changed.

The Eternal Divine Courtyard had been abandoned for a long time...

Sealed by the Time Lock, what was left of the nearly eternal time might remain this way forever, and that would mean endless boring years for them.

Although no one said it out loud, deep in their hearts, they all hoped that something would break this stagnant eternal state. And now, this strange thing appeared.

Divine Farmer stared pensively at Zen, who was carried on the brass man's shoulder.

Even though he couldn't figure out what was going on, he now fully understood why the Element Spirit race wanted to win Zen over.

But he'd gone this far, so he didn't intend to give up.

With a slight wave of his right hand, the already twisted Divine Farmer Ruler was hidden inside his body.

Swoosh! A terrifying bloodline power was released from Divine Farmer's body. A split second later, a green, horned, bull-headed shadow appeared behind him.

The shadow let out a strange cry and disappeared in an instant. The moment it disappeared, it started materializing within Divine Farmer's body.

In addition to using their own bloodline to condense a lifeblood weapon, Eternal Realm warriors also had their own bloodline theurgies.

For example, the golden sword of Eastern Emperor Taiyi and the Nine-Sun World Destruction of Emperor Charm were both their bloodline therugies.

Divine Farmer named his bloodline "Weird Blood". As one of the root-level bloodlines, the Weird Blood was extremely powerful, not at all inferior to the bloodline belonged to Yellow Thearch, Eastern Emperor Taiyi, Emperor Charm, or other Eternal Realm warriors.

However, very few people in the Source World had seen the bloodline theurgy of Divine Farmer because he very rarely used it.

The Weird Blood could transform him into three different mutants, which were all indestructible. During the transformation process, however, Divine Farmer's consciousness would be hazy. Moreover, the more he used his blood theurgy, the longer he would stay in his mutant form.

He was worried that one day, he might lose the ability to transform back to his original form and become a strange monster without wisdom, so he was very careful in using this bloodline theurgy of his.

In fact, he didn't want to use his bloodline theurgy in handling the members of the Black Ship.

Nevertheless, upon seeing the strange characteristics of Zen's body, he felt the urgency to activate his blood theurgy.

His body began to lengthen, and two horns grew on his head. His feet also turned into a pair of strong hooves...

It was a mutant in the form of a goat monster... Divine Farmer's consciousness was gradually fading.

The goat monster was the most ferocious of his three mutant forms, but it was also the form that Divine Farmer hated the least.

The only thing that Divine Farmer could do to control this goat monster was to plant a purpose in his mind—he must take Zen back.

A second later, the consciousness in the goat monster's eyes completely disappeared. After a moment of haziness, it let out a strange howl.

The brass man standing not far away had been observing for a long time.

Seeing that the goat monster was still a little confused, he immediately carried Zen and smashed at the monster with Zen's body.

"Boom!"

The strike still contained a force of three hundred thousand divine megatons.

While the goat monster was still howling, it was directly thrown down from the air, creating a huge crater in the ground.

However, the almost indestructible goat monster suffered no injury at all. It turned over, ran a few steps on the ground with both hands and feet, and pounced on the brass man.

"Boom!"

With Zen on his shoulder, the brass man once again smashed Zen towards the ground. He didn't believe that the mutant transformed from Divine Farmer wouldn't really be killed.

However, what the brass man didn't know was that every time he carried Zen and smashed him, the third light column in the area symbolizing destruction under the sacred cup in the Eternal Divine Courtyard would grow taller.

Chapter 3860 The Creation Quadrant The light pillar in the destruction quadrant continued to rise.

Soon, it touched the ring of light at the very edge of the map.

The four bronze statues all looked upon the cup.

Now that there were three light pillars, Zen was supposedly ready to wake up.

He obtained the ancestry-level bloodline so easily! Yet he remained lying motionless in the sacred cup.

The bronze statues had no clue that Zen was also confused.

As he lay in the darkness, he was positive that he was awake and not in a dream.

But he couldn't feel himself at all. At the very least, his sense of touch and smell had already left. He couldn't even perceive if he had a corporeal body —it seemed as though he was floating in the darkness as a mere lonely soul.

Fortunately, the soul's eyes and ears remained intact—Zen could see dots of light in the distance, as well as hear some sounds from his surroundings.

Murmurs rang in his ears every now and then. Each time a sound came through, the dots of light would spread out like dancing flies.

It seemed like there was someone chanting incantations… and the light dots were following the commands of said incantations.

Why was such a thing in his mind, Zen wondered? How long would the state last? He received no answer.

Meanwhile, in the Source World… something explosive resounded.

A pit that could hold a great lake suddenly appeared—the brass man smashed into the ground.

At the bottom of the pit, as soon as the goat monster's body was exposed, it was thrown into the air and smacked back down by the brass man.

"Boom!"

Another great pit appeared as the goat monster was once again smashed into the ground. Behind them, there were already over twenty lake-sized huge pits.

While the brass man's series of attacks caused no substantial damage to the goat monster, the latter was at least sufficiently suppressed enough so it had no strength to fight back.

But with each strike, the brass man released three hundred thousand divine megatons of force, enough that the other two Black Ship members could hardly bear it any longer.

The Withering Power and the Power Transfer Lens were both Other Shore Tokens from Stage Thirty-three of the Other Shore, but they consumed divine crystals rapidly.

At such a consumption rate, it was impractical to crumb divine crystals one after another to replenish the Other Shore Tokens. A single replenishment of such a level cost millions of divine crystals.

Even if the powerful warriors of the Holy Soul Realm were extremely agile, they couldn't possibly crush all the crystals one by one.

Before entering a battle, they usually prepared a space ring where they collected the many crushed divine crystals—this way, they could replenish their Other Shore Token with divine crystal energy during the battle.

But the brass man had used the force far too extravagantly.

Once the Black Ship members replenished divine crystal energy three consecutive times, the spare space ring was already empty.

"Shera!"

"Edith!"

The Black Ship members shifted their eyes to the two, pointing to them at the same time.

Both Shera and Edith immediately understood what they meant and instantly moved to the front of the two, giving them their spare space rings.

And so there was a break during the transfer.

The brass man was pouring his force into the goat monster's body through Zen, but there was now a sudden break in the force's steady stream.

As a result, the brass man attacked with only a few thousand divine megatons of force.

"Bang!"

The goat monster struck a pose, ready to be thrown out again.

Suddenly, it found the impact on it far too gentle and weak.

It glared at the brass man in surprise.

When the man looked back at it, his eyes were filled with the same expression.

Realizing that the brass man lost his strength, its two horns began flashing green light before immediately lowering its head to push the man up with just its horns.

Each time the Divine Farmer turned into a goat monster, it would kill many people. With its ferocious personality, it refused to stop until it killed the brass man.

Seeing the horns rushing toward him, the brass man was so anxious that he lifted Zen up, using him as a shield to cover him.

The Divine Farmer ordered the goat monster to take Zen back before his consciousness disappeared.

But the goat monster didn't seem to care one bit about what the Divine Farmer was thinking whatsoever. Instead, it rushed right at Zen's head.

"Crack!"

The collision's great impact sent both Zen and the brass man into the air.

Because of the "Combat Dragon Absorb", the brass man was still firmly gripping Zen when the latter once again displayed something miraculous— he was left completely unharmed from the goat monster's attack.

"Woo..."

After having taken quite many beatings from the brass man, the goat monster didn't care to show any mercy toward him now that it finally had its chance for revenge.

As its pair of strong and powerful rear legs made a leap, its sharp horns with green light pierced toward the brass man once again.

In terms of real strength, even powerful existences such as Fuxi and Yellow Thearch couldn't defeat the goat monster too easily—let alone the brass man who was only at the Holy Soul Realm.

Knowing that he couldn't defeat the goat monster, the brass man had no choice but to place his hopes on Zen, tightly placing him in front to serve as a shield.

"Crack!"

"Crack!"

"Crack!"

Because of the goat monster's repeated attacks, another light pillar extended from the quadrant that represented "creation" at the bottom of the sacred cup—it was exactly the same as the one in the destruction quadrant, rising upward.

The four bronze statues believed Zen would stop. But they were left dumbfounded again in the face of the new light pillar.

"This light pillar can also reach consummation?"

The root-level bloodline that the Divine Farmer inherited was initially born from the creation quadrant.

The very fact that he had turned himself into a goat monster was a form of creation.

From its appearance, strength could be displayed in thousands of billions of forms, but in the map of the ancestry-level bloodline, strength would be simply divided into four great quadrants: destruction, creation, life, and space-time. Only small differences existed among the three hundred seventy-three light pillars that focused on various areas.

The goat monster's attacks directly helped Zen consummate a light pillar.

Once it launched over ten attacks in a single shot, the two Black Ship members finally replenished enough divine crystal energy.

Chapter 3861 Unable To Leave This was the captain's style of doing things. He always completed tasks at minimum cost.

Chapter 3862 Gap Of Strength It was because of the Chaos Ancient Gods that the Black Ship had spent their days sailing endlessly, never settling down in the Source World.

Meanwhile, Yellow Thearch was also preoccupied, running as fast as he could along the boundary wall.

After you joined the Element Spirit race, you unconsciously slacked off on cultivation. How much do you know about the Three Purities Stage?"

Some time ago, Fuxi, Yellow Thearch, and Divine Farmer were all roughly on the same level of strength. Back then, it never would've crossed Fuxi's mind that he would defeat Yellow Thearch with ease.

It was because he had chosen to take the rougher path that he had grown stronger than the other masters at the Eternal Realm.

Chapter 3863 A Huge Figure Back then, Fuxi had challenged Gerald, but he failed. In turn, Gerald had taught him a hard lesson.

What made it more impressive for Gerald was that even though he was in a bad situation at that time, he was still able to defeat Fuxi.

Generally speaking, the Chaos Ancient Gods were the foundation of the chaos. Once they participated in the mortal battles, the situation would become quite complicated.

According to Yellow Thearch's plan, they were supposed to abduct Zen while they helped Usman increase his strength. If they successfully executed both, then the Bearing race and the Divine Farmer race would be forever invincible! However, things didn't go smoothly. Now that Othniel was directly involved in the battle, they might have to do everything in advance before they made full preparations.

But no matter what, he was already invincible because Othniel coated him with a layer of space membrane.

Swish! Yellow Thearch slashed Fuxi with his sword once more, and Fuxi dodged it using his fast speed instead of the spatial transference.

Although he successfully evaded one strike, he couldn't dodge all the follow-up strikes.

In only a short amount of time, Fuxi acquired several horrible wounds, and half of his face had gotten disfigured. He looked miserable.

"So much for that!"

Yellow Thearch's eyes glinted coldly, and then three more holy ways gathered on his sword.

For him, Fuxi was just like an immovable target. If he couldn't even deal with Fuxi in this situation, he would be worthless.

Buzz...

As his sword, which contained three holy ways sounded, innumerable sword shadows flew towards Fuxi at full speed.

Just when he thought that Fuxi was powerless now, the latter's aura suddenly changed.

A bright green beam of light lit up his eyes, as if an immensely powerful life force was infused into his body. All of his severe wounds healed in a second.

The green light only lasted for a while, and then it turned red. His aura also became quite aggressive.

Whoosh! In the next moment, he swiftly pounced on Yellow Thearch.

Even if Yellow Thearch had the protection of the space membrane, a chill ran down his spine.

Instead of swinging his sword to fight back, he instinctively dodged and retreated.

Crack! The space membrane that covered him exploded, and then his left arm was ripped off by Fuxi.

Still, his decision to retreat saved his life. Had he relied on the space membrane and counterattacked, Fuxi could've killed him.

He pulled a long face once he had landed far away. He also looked up at the sky like Fuxi did before. What he had been worried about really happenedanother Chaos Ancient God had a hand in their affair.

Just then, a giant scorpion shadow appeared in the Separate Amber Province and other hundreds of provinces, including the Bloom Divine Province and the Pear Hill.

Many creatures raised their heads to look at the enormous scorpion, and all of them had mixed feelings: first was that they felt deeply attached to the scorpion, and second was they also feared it, as if it would destroy them right then and there.

Gerald was the Chaos Ancient God who controlled the truth of life. In the early days of the Source World, Gerald could interfere with the cycle of life and even create creatures. Therefore, it was safe to say that all living creatures in the current chaos originated from him.

Furthermore, he was the ruler of all living creatures. Not only could he create lives, but he could destroy them too.

As soon as Gerald's figure appeared, another enormous figure also emerged on the other side. It was a gigantic one-eyed monster with a strange stooping body.

It was none other than Othniel, who had coated Yellow Thearch with a layer of space membrane.

"Haven't you figured it out yet?" Othniel's voice echoed throughout the hundreds of provinces.

The Chaos Ancient Gods also had their stands.

From their perspective, the Purge Way was clearly in line with their interests. That was why Othniel was willing to help Yellow Thearch.

Despite that, Othniel didn't want to fight with Gerald. They both came from the last chaotic era, and although they belonged to different races, their races got along well with each other at that time.

Therefore, he still tried to persuade Gerald to stand with him even now.

It even didn't want to go back to its master. In its own way, it wanted to be a special No. 9527, not just a soul fragment.

As soon as No. 9527 spoke this, the brain masters surrounding Gerald broke into indignant chaos.

Although Zen on his own was extraordinary, with the help of No. 9527, he was able to reach greater heights.

However, just as he felt like he couldn't be any more impressed, he reached the part where Zen entered the Eternal Scroll Painting. He became more stunned! All this happened in the span of seconds. In the blink of an eye, Gerald had fully understood what No. 9527 and Zen had been through together. He gently shut his huge eyes, and then opened them again slowly, as he felt conflicting emotions rage within him.

Zen's performance was completely beyond his expectations, and even beyond his imagination...

Previously, Gerald had been a little hesitant, but at this moment, he no longer had any misgivings.

"I understand now," Gerald's voice rang out in the air, and it was easily transmitted to the ears of all the creatures from over a hundred provinces, sounding very peaceful. "Let go of Zen and retreat. Then we can forget what happened today."

Instantly, his aura became menacingly strong.

Othniel's single eye shook wildly.

Othniel had the highest space authority in the chaos. Now that he couldn't reach a consensus with Gerald, he planned to exile him.

Once the blue light disappeared, so did Gerald.

Othniel's laughter roared throughout the skies.

However, even under his pull, Zen remained unmoved.

His invincible space truth had no effect at this moment! Chapter 3865 The Descending Man In Black The captain of the Black Ship, Shera, and the others also stared at the brass man, feeling quite confounded.

"Do you need any help?"

Crack! He stretched out his feet and kicked up against the transparent wall of the Invisible Ship. It seemed unnervingly easy for him to do that. The ship shook violently and stopped shrinking.

He gently hitched up his robe and flew upwards like a black goshawk. At the same time, a rumbling sound echoed from the sky. A terrifying energy quietly swept past and then disappeared without a trace. This was the punishment of truth that could not descend.

Othniel didn't think the members of the Black Ship would ever escape. In his mind, it was inconceivable they would be able to escape from the Invisible Ship.

After he had dealt with the Black Ship, there were only two targets of the Pear Hill remaining.

Since he made his move, he would not let any of his targets escape.

But moments after he left the ship, he felt a huge movement coming from behind him.

Othniel turned around and saw the man in black. His cold eyes flashed a trace of seriousness.

In the chaos, even the strongest Eternal Realm warrior couldn't oppose the Chaos Ancient Gods who controlled the truth. Therefore, even Fuxi and the Black Ship had not been taken seriously by Othniel. At least, Othniel felt that these Eternal Realm warriors posed no threat to him.

However, the man in black who had now appeared made Othniel feel an instinctive vigilance. This vigilance only happened when he was facing other Chaos Ancient Gods. He didn't expect that he would have such a feeling when facing a mere human, and this left him feeling a little confused.

Fuxi and the Snake Goddess, who had been pulled here by Othniel, quietly exchanged nervous looks.

Of course, they knew that the man in black had descended from the Other Shore and must be a member of the Nihility race. However, the members of the Nihility race always took mysterious and unpredictable actions, and they were unable to determine the man in black's identity.

In fact, not long ago, the man in black had appeared in Stage Thirty-two of the Other Shore. If Pearce had been present, he would have been able to recognize him.

However, if the Nihility race could duel Othniel to the death, Fuxi and the others would celebrate seeing it.

"Who are you?" asked Othniel.

The man in black sniffed the air, revealing some enjoyment on his face.

"I've been looking forward to this moment for a long time. Even though more than a thousand chaotic eras have passed, the scent of this world still hasn't changed,"

the man in black said without answering Othniel's question. Othniel's face darkened, and he asked in a low voice, "Tell me who you are!"

As he spoke, he suddenly lashed out at the man in black, and a crescentshaped space crack hurtled straight towards the man in black. The space crack that the Chaos Ancient God had so casually created was extremely lethal.

Facing the space crack, the man in black smiled faintly and extended his palm to block the crack as if swatting a fly.

Sizzle...

When the man's palm met the space crack, a grating noise sounded, and the space crack disintegrated.

"Not in your wildest dreams," responded Othniel.

If it weren't for the fact that Zen was able to absorb all the energy and couldn't be transported away, Othniel would have hidden Zen in a corner of the chaos as he had done to Gerald.

If Othniel had done so, it wouldn't matter how strong the man in black was.

Finding a human in the vast chaos was like looking for a needle in a haystack.

Chapter 3866 Blind Spots The eyes of the man in black clothes were devoid of emotions.

When people looked at him, they got an impression of a tightened bow simmering with a surging power that could be released any time.

His emotions were like deep water in a tranquil lake. He looked outwardly composed, as if he was merely taking a walk in his courtyard. But everyone could sense that there was great power concealed below the surface.

No one could see through his real thoughts, not even Othniel.

Othniel's power on the other hand, was an excellent option. Every time Othniel used the power of space against Zen, Zen's body immediately devoured it.

"Since what you've grasped is only a part of the space truth, you also have blind spots in space."

The man's voice echoed again. Othniel lifted the space saber but discovered that he couldn't determine the direction of the voice this time. Since the cyan light was only as thick as a little finger, it didn't create a hole large enough for the chaotic energy from the outside to flow into the Source World. But it had killed innumerable innocent creatures on its way out.

The small wound wasn't much trouble for Othniel. He only felt a slight pain in his back, and he brought his saber down behind him a few more times.

Chapter 3867 Direct Exile Generally speaking, the self-healing ability of the space in the Source World was quite strong.

Countless figures flashed inside the space blocks. Those figures were the man in black.

The man in black did not disappear. Instead, he moved at an incredible speed.

According to the common space rules, one had to create a short distance or even a long distance space channel for the Grand Teleportation or instant teleportation. Only then could they cross from one end to the other end of the space channel.

However, the man in black didn't need to do that. He could appear at any point then disappear at another point on his accord.

Even Othniel couldn't do such a thing.

"You can't possibly refract all my sword radiance, nor can you stay cautious all the time. Just three sword strikes are enough. It's impressive to kill a Son of Truth with three sword strikes," the man in black said from the space.

As he spoke, his sword released more concentrated cyan sword radiance.

The long sword radiance, which was as thick as a finger, was like a thick thread. While Othniel was at the center, it refracted in all directions like mad.

In this way, the mighty warriors of the Eternal Realm, including the Snake Goddess, Fuxi, and Mahoney, were in a more dangerous situation. The sword radiance came and pierced through them from time to time, and they almost couldn't dodge it.

Only Yellow Thearch remained unharmed because he placed Zen above his head as a natural shield.

Crack! Like the man in black had said, Othniel couldn't be careful all the time.

Although he could refract ninety-nine point nine percent of the cyan sword radiance away, there would always be a little cyan sword light left as time went by.

Finally, one ray of cyan sword radiance dodged Othniel's refraction and punctured his shoulder.

"The second sword strike." The voice of the man in black came again.

Othniel's face darkened.

The man in black had just said that he could kill him with three sword strikes.

Based on the cyan light's lethality, not even thirty or three hundred strikes could cause any substantial damage to him, let alone only three strikes.

Yet, according to the man in black, there might be some other consequences if the cyan light hit him thrice. Or was it just a threat? The Three Purities Stage was a magical place with all kinds of strange abilities.

At first, Othniel wanted to deal with the man in black slowly while he tried to come up with a solution—but after he felt that things had gotten much worse, he suddenly looked ferocious.

His eyes suddenly turned into two weird blue energy entities and abruptly exploded. At the same time, a large block appeared covering dozens of miles around the man in black.

Then the block disappeared, together with the man inside it.

Chapter 3868 Uncle A space which was thirty miles wide, thirty miles high, and thirty miles long had been deleted from the chaos and exiled into the Deleting Space.

On all sides, everything squeezed into the gap to fill in the disappeared space. The ground itself was pulled up. A majestic mountain, thirty miles high, appeared out of thin air.

The last time, Zen had quickly returned after Mount exiled him. This attracted Othniel's attention.

The outside world thought that the Land of Ashes—also known as the Deleting Space—was controlled by Othniel. In fact, he couldn't affect anything in the Deleting Space.

The information left by the Sons of Truth on the Other Shore seemed to indicate that the Deleting Space was under the control of Othniel. But much had changed over the past few hundred chaotic eras. The Deleting Space had undergone a dramatic transformation, and Othniel had lost control of it.

He didn't know for certain what had happened inside.

All he knew was that he had the ability to exile people and things into the Deleting Space. However, he had no power to delete the creatures and things within that space.

Zen's safe return from the Deleting Space had shaken Othniel. He immediately tried to invade the Deleting Space to reclaim his authority over it.

None of Othniel's attempts to regain control was successful.

Othniel had always felt that something strange was in the Deleting Space, something that he could not track or detect. It was a sore spot in his heart.

In this case, Othniel would not have chosen to delete the man in black unless he had no other choice. After all, it might prove ineffective.

However, since the man in black had been deleted, Othniel seized this opportunity to take Zen away.

The man in black frowned as he floated in the Deleting Space.

He raised a hand to pat his head, muttering, "I was too careless. I forgot this trick."

It was not a good thing for him to be exiled to this damned place.

He had come with the help of the Descending Ring, but now the Descending Ring had grown dim. He had lost contact with the Other Shore.

What if he was truly trapped in this cursed space, unable to find his way out? It would cause enormous problems for the Nihility race.

As he floated, the man in black suddenly realized the strangeness of his situation. "Shouldn't the things in the Deleting Space be completely destroyed? Why is this place..."

To his surprise, after some time, he noticed something visible in the distance. He squinted. It seemed to be a vast, endless, floating wasteland.

He stared at this unexpected sight, feeling more confused than ever. His eyes widened when he saw two figures flying in his direction. One was Ziya, and the other was Geoffrey.

At first the man in black doubted if it was truly Ziya. But when he confirmed the truth of Ziya's identity, twin flames began burning in his eyes.

When he was facing Othniel, a powerful Chaos Ancient God, he had managed to act cool and collected, as though nothing had happened.

But when he saw Ziya, the man in black could no longer restrain the anger that had burned in his heart for countless years. His gaze was filled with killing intent.

A low buzz sounded as he attacked.

He tapped the Cyan Misty Sword, and a thin ray of cyan light shot towards Ziya.

Not long after Ziya and Geoffrey returned, a loud noise could be heard coming from the Deleting Space.

This was a common occurrence, so Ziya didn't take it seriously. He brought Geoffrey directly there to see what was going on.

But before he had even noticed the man in black, he saw the extremely sharp and deadly ray of cyan light rushing towards him.

His eyes narrowed when he sensed the power of the cyan light. He instantly waved his hand, and a golden whip lashed out like a poisonous dragon at the ray of cyan light.

The golden and cyan lights converged in midair. Ziya waved his golden whip, forming many small spirals, and soon the cyan light was swallowed up.

Geoffrey hung back, watching the attack and counterattack with surprise.

He had always considered Ziya to be much stronger than his father.

Despite the fact that he was powerless in the Abstruse Energy World, Ziya had never met an opponent in the chaos. He had a grim look on his face that Geoffrey had not seen before.

Geoffrey caught sight of the man in black and wondered who he was. Why had he initiated a fight with Ziya as soon as he arrived, without even speaking to him first? But the fight was not over.

Rays of cyan light shot out from afar, and some of them headed straight for Geoffrey.

Ziya's face turned cold. His lips formed a sneer as he raised the golden whip in his hand and flicked it, causing a loud explosion in midair. The whip reformed into an arc of bright golden light which lashed towards the cyan rays.

The previously invincible cyan lights seemed fragile compared to the golden lights.

Every time a golden light bloomed, a cyan ray was drawn away, turning into a cyan lotus that slowly dissipated into space.

The cyan rays blasted towards Ziya one after another, and he lashed out at each one with his golden whip.

In the span of a few seconds, thirty-six rays of golden light bloomed, and thirty-six cyan lotuses appeared and dissipated.

The fierce clash of energy was a spectacular, dazzling scene. Geoffrey watched with great fascination. He knew that although the colorful bursts of energy were beautiful, they were also terrifying. A single ray of light could kill him instantly.

His estimation of Ziya rose, and he now believed more than ever that Ziya was immensely powerful.

Although all his attacks had been dispersed, the man in black seemed undaunted. He raised his Cyan Misty Sword once more. Six black flags appeared behind him.

Thin black energy lines flowed on the surface of each flag.

These were known as the Six Soul Flags.

Ziya raised an eyebrow. He called out, "Are you really planning to fight me to the death, uncle?"

The Cyan Misty Sword trembled in the man's hand. He drew a circle from top to bottom with himself at the center. Although there was no wind, the Six Soul Flags fluttered, and a mysterious and indescribable aura spread out from his body. He shouted back, "You have the cheek to call me uncle?"

Again, a buzz signaled his impending attack.

The black energy emanated by the Six Soul Flags suddenly flowed inward, gathering on the surface of the Cyan Misty Sword. The cyan glow of the sword intersected with the black energy, and the sword began to burn.

Raising his sword, the man in black rushed towards Ziya.

Ziya gently pushed Geoffrey, and an unseen force propelled Geoffrey away.

In the face of such a powerful attack, he had no time to protect Geoffrey.

"Let bygones be bygones. Why do you still keep the past in mind?" Ziya said, lifting his own golden whip once more.

Ziya's God Lashing Whip had been created by the Primeval Lord of Heaven with Ziya's root-level bloodline. It was his most powerful weapon.

"Your master has said the same thing many times," the man in black said coldly. "It is nonsense!"

He was the Grandmaster of Heaven whom Zen had met.

He and the Primeval Lord of Heaven had learned from the same master, so he was Ziya's uncle.

At first, Ziya had not known if he was still alive. After all, when the 77th chaos ended, Ziya had been exiled to the Deleting Space.

Ziya didn't know anything about what happened later on the Other Shore until Zen took him out from the Deleting Space.

Although Ziya had grown much since those days, he still found it deeply unsettling that the mere sight of him had spurred the Grandmaster of Heaven to an immediate fight to the death.

Chapter 3869 Passing The Ball Within the 77th chaos, there had been a great conflict between the Interception Sect, created by the Grandmaster of Heaven, and the Enlightenment Sect, created by the Primeval Lord of Heaven. The reason behind this conflict was also related to the Finale Way.

At the end of the battle, the Grandmaster of Heaven had been defeated by Ziya, and the foundation of the Interception Sect had been destroyed beyond repair.

The Grandmaster of Heaven had led the remaining people of their sect to the Other Shore in an attempt to escape, and there they had quickly disappeared. In the past hundreds of chaotic eras, no one had ever seen the Grandmaster of Heaven himself, or the members of the Interception Sect.

It was not until the Nihility race appeared out of the blue that the Grandmaster of Heaven began to show his face once again.

There was no known knowledge of what the Grandmaster of Heaven had gone through, or how he had become the leader of the Nihility race during that time.

The moment Ziya had descended into the Bloom Divine Province, the Primeval Lord of Heaven had warned him of the Grandmaster of Heaven, and to be cautious if he were to ever come across him. The latter had not moved on from when the Interception Sect had been destroyed.

Ziya hadn't felt the need to take the words seriously at the time. He had thought that time would ease the pain, and erase the hatred in the Grandmaster of Heaven's heart. However, when they had come across one another in the Deleting Space, fury and hatred had burned in the Grandmaster of Heaven's eyes as he looked at Ziya, regarding him as if they were old enemies.

A metallic 'whoosh' had cut through the air.

With the Cyan Misty Sword in hand, the Grandmaster of Heaven had rushed towards Ziya.

The Six Soul Flags in the distance quivered, and the black fire licking along the blade burned with heavy violence.

Ziya understood just how powerful the Six Soul Flags were. He also knew that the Grandmaster of Heaven had led the Nihility race to great power, and that they could easily stand up to the Elemental Spirit race as near equals. His strength had grown exponentially.

"God Lashing Whip!"

Ziya struck out hard with his whip as he retreated.

The resounding cracks caused by the whip were ear-piercing.

As shadows danced and shimmied along the whip, the void began to tremble. What looked to be ripples appeared in the air, warping and distorting everything within their sight.

The movement of the God Lashing Whip was erratic, and had no pattern to follow as it sent golden shadows one after another into the void.

Those countless shadows then melded together to create a long, narrow dragon shadow that immediately rushed the Grandmaster of Heaven.

The shadows seemed alive, sizzling and cracking as they moved.

The Grandmaster of Heaven thrust his sword in front of him and shifted forward. The black flames soared high, and ate away the golden shadows from the whip as they approached.

When he had advanced to only a few dozen feet away from Ziya, Ziya relinquished his hold on his God Lashing Whip and bowed to the Grandmaster of Heaven with cupped hands.

The Grandmaster of Heaven paused, confused by the gesture. His eyes flashed with anger before turning cold. "Do you think this display will make me show mercy? Ziya, how naive you are!"

"No, I did not think you would show me mercy. Now is not the time for us to fight. I'm sorry that I have to do this to you," Ziya said quietly.

"What?"

The Grandmaster of Heaven found himself thoroughly confused, and the sudden sensation of the sky and earth moving made his head spin. In the next moment, he appeared in the Separate Amber Province. This was where Othniel had exiled him.

Ziya had total control over the Deleting Space. He had more authority than the Chaos Ancient God here. Not only could he freely dispose of things within the space, he could also find the same time node.

It wasn't that Ziya didn't have the strength to battle the Grandmaster of Heaven, but he shared the same thought as his master, the Primeval Lord of Heaven. When they had defeated the Interception Sect, they had felt some modicum of guilt and did not want to fight him because of that.

The moment the right space and time node had been found, Ziya sent the Grandmaster of Heaven out of the Deleting Space.

Once Othniel had exiled the Grandmaster of Heaven into the Deleting Space, he floated down. He worried that the Grandmaster of Heaven would return quickly, so he planned to take Zen away as soon as possible.

But before he could descend, a space fluctuation occurred not far away, and the Grandmaster of Heaven emerged.

Othniel's face contorted slightly before smoothing back out. Without hesitation, he slashed his hand through the air in the direction of the Grandmaster of Heaven, and immediately wrapped him in another expanse of space.

The Grandmaster of Heaven found himself still in a daze after being forced out of the Deleting Space. It made no sense. How did Ziya have such an ability? While he was stuck within his cloud of confusion, a space fluctuation enveloped him flawlessly and he found himself once more in the Deleting Space.

Ziya couldn't find the words to express his own confusion. Within a span of several seconds, the Grandmaster of Heaven had been cast out only to be returned moments later.

What the hell was going on? With his intelligence, it was not difficult for Ziya to grasp what was exactly going on.

The only possible explanation could be that when the Grandmaster of Heaven descended through the Descending Ring, he had fought with the Son of Truth who controlled that particular space.

Ziya could have never guessed that the reason the two fought was Zen.

"You'd best vent all that anger on the Son of Truth," Ziya grumbled.

With a wave of his hand, he sent the Grandmaster of Heaven back out.

Othniel though, who was in the Separate Amber Province, was on his guard. The moment he saw the Grandmaster of Heaven was cast out, he began to delete the space.

With no time to react, the Grandmaster of Heaven was sent right back to the Deleting Space. He felt as if he were going to be sick...

Ziya sighed, his shoulders slumping. The Grandmaster of Heaven might be difficult to deal with, and the Son of Truth probably had no choice but to continue to send him back, but it was not a good idea to keep throwing him back and forth like a ball.

"I suppose all I can do is close the Deleting Space."

Over countless chaotic eras, Ziya had managed the affairs and taken over the rights of the Deleting Space. He certainly had the ability to refuse the space that the Son of Truth had "deleted" to enter.

However, Ziya needed the substances that were sent in, one after the other, from the chaos. It allowed him to learn things from within the chaos.

A soft whooshing sound startled Ziya from his thoughts.

The Grandmaster of Heaven had regained his senses enough to utilize Grand Teleportation and reach Ziya instantly.

He raised his hand and swung his sword! The black radiance along the edges of his sword was as bright as fire, and came barreling towards Ziya's face.

Ziya though was a little bit faster...

Before the attack could plow into him, the Grandmaster of Heaven disappeared.

Ziya turned quickly to look at the Deleting Pillars at the far end of the Deleting Space. He waved his hands before him, and a portion of the Deleting Pillars hummed to life with a bright light before quickly dimming.

With that action, the rules of the Deleting Space had changed. There was a unique space node at the entrance of the Deleting Space, and it so happened to be controlled by Othniel. However, Ziya had long ago changed it to be one way, so people could enter but not leave.

But now that particular rule had changed. People could neither enter nor leave.

When the Grandmaster of Heaven had been sent out once more, Othniel immediately enveloped him with space and began to delete it.

However, the space did not disappear, no matter how hard Othniel willed it to.

The Grandmaster of Heaven remained where he had appeared, and stared at Othniel with a puzzled expression.

Could a Chaos Ancient God even make a mistake? "What have you done?! I can't sense the Deleting Space!" Othniel cried in shock.

Losing the ability to delete meant losing a trump card, but usually Chaos Ancient Gods had many of those up their sleeves.

The fact that the ability he had obtained from the space of truth was weakened or muted by another made him feel on edge, the horrible feeling creeping up his spine.

Chapter 3870 The Heart-piercing Lock The Grandmaster of Heaven had already readied himself to enter the Deleting Space once more when Othniel said something strange to him. A visible frown appeared on his face as he stared back at Othniel.

In the eyes of the Grandmaster of Heaven, his opponents on both sides needed to be personally dealt with.

As he was expelled in the Deleting Space that was controlled by Ziya, he was surprised when he observed that the time node could be directly changed.

When he was being transferred between the two places, all he thought about was how he could defeat Ziya.

In his mind, if he could replace Ziya who was controlling the Deleting Space, then he could earn a lot from it. Most importantly, he could also return to the chaos through the time node.

"I didn't do anything. If you want, you can try again," the Grandmaster of Heaven responded with a straight face.

While Othniel heard these words, a strange expression glimmered in his eyes. He took a few steps forward and sneered, "Are you mocking me?"

"No. Of course not," the Grandmaster of Heaven quickly replied. "I'm just hoping that you can try sending me back into that space again."

Seeing the sincere expression of the Grandmaster of Heaven, all of the Eternal Realm warriors that were currently present couldn't help but look at each other with confused faces.

Right now, the Grandmaster of Heaven had a rough estimate of Ziya's abilities.

It seemed that Othniel wasn't pretending. Ziya had most probably shut down the Deleting Space.

Now, the Grandmaster of Heaven was more interested in this magical place and yearned for it even more.

However, Othniel couldn't understand what the Grandmaster of Heaven was really thinking. He tried several times, but the space around the Grandmaster of Heaven was just constantly shaking and there was no way to send him in.

With all that was happening, Othniel couldn't help but ask him, "Tell me.

What exactly happened in that space?"

The Grandmaster of Heaven shrugged and said, "Ha, I can't tell you that."

Of course, he didn't have the slightest intention of telling Othniel the matter about Ziya.

"All right then. I'll know after I kill you." Othniel's voice suddenly became cold. He had a strong urge to figure out what had truly happened in the Deleting Space.

Suddenly, the cubic space surrounding the Grandmaster of Heaven transformed into a solid cube.

Othniel controlled the space truth. With it, he could define and manipulate most of the spaces in the chaos. This time, he controlled the space containing the Grandmaster of Heaven and transformed it into a solid state.

Crash! With a wave of his hand, the whole cube instantly collapsed.

If it was an ordinary Eternal Realm warrior, they would be completely shattered along with the crushed space fragments.

However, the Grandmaster of Heaven was fully prepared, and he was powerful enough not to be easily defeated by such kind of move.

When the view became clear, all they saw were broken space fragments.

The body of the Grandmaster of Heaven couldn't be seen anywhere.

Othniel instantly felt a shiver creeping beneath his skin, as if some dangerous beast was glaring at him somewhere in the dark. Suddenly, the Grandmaster of Heaven appeared above his head.

He was holding a long sword that was pointed downwards, like a praying swordsman. The tip of the sword immediately dashed downwards in an attempt to directly stab Othniel's head.

At the same time, a blue light flashed in Othniel's eyes, and the space above his head suddenly became distorted. The long sword that was supposed to stab his head disappeared as it touched the distorted space. Immediately after that, the sword appeared from the side of the Grandmaster of Heaven, directly aimed at his head.

Othniel bent the space and threw the sword back to the Grandmaster of Heaven to stab himself instead.

However, just before the sword thrust through him, the eyes of the Grandmaster of Heaven also beamed with the same blue light. Suddenly, the space beside his head also became distorted. The Cyan Misty Sword that was fast approaching him instantly disappeared. In a split second, a distorted space appeared in front of Othniel's chest, and the sword rushed out with a violent force, thrusting directly towards his chest.

Splat! A ray of cyan light pierced through Othniel from front to back.

A hint of confusion appeared in Othniel's eyes as he slowly looked at the sword stabbing in his chest. Blood was dripping on his mouth as he stared back at the Grandmaster of Heaven. "Only I could distort the space. How did you..."

The truth was many people could actually connect two points in space and create a circular space channel. It was also the case with the space distortion that Othniel created.

However, most temporary channels that were created by ordinary people were unstable. Only Othniel could manipulate and create a distorted space that could deflect a sword strike that had the power of hundreds of thousands of divine megatons.

But it turned out that Othniel wasn't the only one who could do it now, as the Grandmaster of Heaven blatantly used the same powerful skill to attack him. Since Othniel began to fight with this man, there had been several mysterious things he witnessed that he couldn't comprehend.

"You're asking me why I can do that?" the Grandmaster of Heaven spoke as he slowly pulled out his Cyan Misty Sword from Othniel through the distorted spaces. "It's because the truth-level theurgy is not unique to you. I can also grasp it. And you know what? I can grasp more skills from you if I want."

Othniel's eyes narrowed. There was an extreme mixture of surprise and rage on his face.

If their previous battles seemed to be opportunities to test each other's strengths, then now would be the time for a showdown.

The Grandmaster of Heaven's words rang in his ears, and he understood them very well.

They meant that the Grandmaster of Heaven could deprive the abilities of the Chaos Ancient God.

Whether he could really do that or not was still unknown. However, the fact remained that he had just used the same space distortion theurgy as Othniel did.

"You're an arrogant piece of crap, aren't you? Let's see if you really have the ability to do that!"

Othniel roared in anger. His face began to deform, his pair of eyes started to merge into one, and his teeth became sharper. His head was beginning to expand rapidly as he attempted to return to his original form.

The spectating warriors also knew that the two powerful masters would likely transform into their strongest forms if they were determined to have an all-out battle. That meant that Othniel would turn into his original monstrous form, and the Grandmaster of Heaven would use his Wild God Body.

However, much to their surprise, that wasn't the intention of the Grandmaster of Heaven.

He stood in the air and stared at Othniel with a mocking smile.

Suddenly, Othniel's transformation stopped abruptly. It was as if a superior force suppressed the changes that were going on.

"Why would you need to transform? You look good in your human form.

You don't need to become that ugly one-eyed monster."

Then, the Grandmaster of Heaven gently raised his Cyan Misty Sword.

Soon after, three thin threads quietly appeared and turned out to tightly wrap around Othniel's body. Suddenly, the white thin threads grew larger and turned into white jade chains. The other ends of the chains were connected to a small yellow lock that was in the hand of the Grandmaster of Heaven. The lock was exceptionally exquisite, and there were undecipherable Sanskrit words on both sides. It was the Heart-piercing Lock, another powerful magic treasure of the Grandmaster of Heaven.

Previously, the Grandmaster of Heaven had given a hint that three strikes were all it would take him to kill Othniel. These three sword strikes were what activated the Heart-piercing Lock that completely suppressed Othniel's body. Now everything in Othniel's body was locked up, meaning that all his theurgies were sealed. That was why there was no need for him to use the Wild God Power.

On the outside, Othniel looked motionless. But the truth was he was currently in a fierce struggle within his body. He was trying to free himself, but the Heart-piercing Lock was absolutely powerful. He was extremely enraged with the fact that the dignified Chaos Ancient God like him would be defeated by the Grandmaster of Heaven in this way.

The Grandmaster of Heaven knew about Othniel's on-going efforts and struggling, but he didn't pay much attention to it. He just slowly descended while dragging the white jade chains.

Now that he was able to successfully trap Othniel, it was time for him to deal with the other warriors present.

He knew these warriors' high positions and standpoints in the Source World, but it didn't matter to him. Since he couldn't kill the real masters in the Three Purities Stage, he decided to annihilate first these duplicates of them.

Chapter 3871 Backup Plan After the Grandmaster of Heaven descended, he couldn't help but gaze at those down below.

The Snake Goddess, Fuxi, Yellow Thearch, each one of them made his blood boil.

He knew that the people that stood before him had different standpoints and were mere avatars devoid of memory, but it didn't stop the inexplicable hatred that surged in his heart when his eyes swept over their faces.

His negative feelings did not go unnoticed. Everyone felt the waves of anger that emanated from the Grandmaster of Heaven, including Snake Goddess, Fuxi, Yellow Thearch and Divine Farmer who had gradually recovered from the form of a goat monster.

Mahoney, however, felt a bit lucky.

This mysterious man in black had such a furious expression when he looked at the others but when it came to her, all he had was an expressionless gaze.

She hoped she wouldn't find trouble with her.

Just as Mahoney silently rejoiced, the Grandmaster of Heaven turned towards her. "I shall kill this irrelevant person first.

"Buzz!"

The Heart-piercing Lock in his hand trembled just as a long, thin chain emerged and headed straight towards Mahoney. Instead of white jade, the chain was stark black, obviously of lower grade than the one that had trapped Othniel. But it was more than enough to trap Mahoney.

After she heard the Grandmaster of Heaven's words, Mahoney's face quickly paled. She rolled backwards, just as the chain headed her way, and tried to get out of her now precarious situation.

The space in front of the black chain distorted as it appeared right in front of Mahoney.

"Puff!"

Mahoney's armor, a masterpiece that she was quite proud of, shattered underneath the piercing force of the black chain.

With no defensive chestplate, the black chain sunk into her chest, and the moment it entered her body, the Spearhead Armor of Destruction on her body collapsed instantly while her life force rapidly faded away.

In the blink of an eye, Mahoney's life force dissipated entirely.

An Eternal Realm warrior truly was no match against the Grandmaster of Heaven.

As the chain retracted, Mahoney's corpse snapped back and shot towards the black ship.

"Deal with the corpse," the Grandmaster of Heaven muttered darkly.

The sight of Mahoney's corpse made Shera salivate.

Her ghouls were weak and all she could really do was transform her own body.

The Grandmaster of Heaven basically awarded her an Eternal Realm warrior, which meant she had a lot of room to work with when it came to her transformation. In her eyes, Mahoney's body was an extremely rare treasure.

Shera caught her body and gave Fuxi and the others a momentary side glance. "Thank you, Grandmaster of Heaven."

The meaning behind her eyes was clear: these Eternal Realm warriors were next.

If Shera cultivated these warriors into ghouls then she would be able to do anything she wanted in the Source World.

Yellow Thearch's and Divine Farmer's faces darkened when they witnessed Mahoney's end. Meanwhile, Fuxi and the Snake Goddess began to gather their power.

Not long ago, these two groups of people were still fighting each other.

Now there was no other choice out of this situation but to join hands and fight against this powerful enemy! This mysterious man in black was truly strange.

Not only did he possess Othniel's truth-level theurgy which was impossible to guard against, he also had the Heart-piercing Lock that had the ability to entrap and lock everything within its hold.

The Snake Goddess exchanged a knowing look with Fuxi as she summoned a Descending Ring in her hand.

After she obtained the golden red Chaotic Source Spirits from Zen, she carefully studied the use of the Descending Rings.

In the beginning, Fuxi was keen on reserving the Descending Rings to summon the Augury Dog.

The Augury Dog was powerful, and was his best friend in the Three Purities Stage. In terms of strength, he was only a little weaker than Fuxi, and much more powerful than the ordinary warriors at the Eternal Realm.

A Descending Ring was not easy to obtain so why would they use it just so that one more Eternal Realm master could guard the Pear Hill? The Snake Goddess did not want that.

So on the Three Purities Stage, she gave a Descending Ring to the Primal Crocodile race.

They were also an extremely powerful force in the Three Purities Stage but were extremely xenophobic and cared little for the affairs of the world.

Even the Element Spirit race did not dare provoke them, much less enter their territory.

A long time ago, the Snake Goddess saved the life of a little Primal Crocodile and earned her this elusive race's friendship.

With this friendship forged, the leader of the race agreed to the Snake Goddess's request and promised to help her out whenever she needed their support to return the favor.

There was no way she would summon such powerful warriors from the Other Shore if she had any other choice.

This situation was so unexpected. Just a moment ago, everyone was watching the two fighting and then suddenly Othniel was captured and all Eternal Realm warriors had to worry about their fates.

Beside her, Fuxi's eyes remained full of fighting spirit.

Save for the Heart-piercing Lock and a few small theurgies, this man in black wasn't that intimidating. Fuxi figured that if he truly went all out then he could defeat him.

Just as the two were about to make their move, Yellow Thearch's forehead split open and a burst of hearty laughter was heard.

"Grandmaster of Heaven! Why are you in such a hurry to descend from the Other Shore?" It was Claire from the Element Spirit race! There was no surprise on the Grandmaster of Heaven's face when he heard this voice. He'd fought with the Element Spirit race for hundreds of chaotic eras so it would be more surprising if they didn't show up.

A smile broke through his face. "As far as I know, you haven't found a way to descend yet."

Claire scoffed. "That's because they're too stupid."

"It doesn't matter if they are stupid or geniuses. If you don't have backup plans, just shut your mouth and admit that I've won."

After he spoke, the Grandmaster of Heaven lifted his Cyan Misty Sword and stabbed towards Yellow Thearch's forehead.

Yellow Thearch's expression changed and he revealed an incredibly charming smile. "Although we missed the Descending Rings, it doesn't mean we don't have other ways to descend!" he said in a girlish voice.

"Phew!"

Everyone was witness to how Yellow Thearch's hair suddenly burned and the eyeball in the center of his forehead glowed with a golden light that emitted an aura similar to that of Descending Rings.

They watched as his appearance, expression, and aura, all transformed into Claire's image.

Before the Grandmaster of Heaven could react, Claire had already stepped forward and swung Zen towards him, hard.

"Buzz!"

A burst of blue light flashed in the Grandmaster of Heaven's eyes as he used the spatial distortion to dodge the blow.

"Damn it!"

"Grandmaster..."

"That Zen can devour..."

The people from the Black Ship all tried to warn him but it was already too late.

The moment Zen touched the twisted space, he completely devoured the energy and returned the space to normal which meant he smashed onto the Grandmaster of Heaven with no hindrance whatsoever.

"Puff!"

Hit by such a formidable weapon, the Grandmaster of Heaven was sent flying into the air.

Claire smirked in satisfaction at this temporary weapon of hers.

"Fire!"

Sizzle! She wanted to ignite a flame but forgot the characteristics of Zen's body.

The fire barely flickered as it was immediately absorbed by him.

She made a face but did not really care. She took a step forward and reached the other side of the space. Again, she wielded Zen as a blunt weapon.

"Bang!"

As Zen's body smashed onto the Grandmaster of Heaven the second time, Othniel, who was bound by the Heart-piercing Lock, was also dragged down and hit the ground hard.

Chapter 3872 Swallow The Separate Amber Province looked like a rag. As the two fought, it began rolling, wrinkling, and tearing.

Creatures that resided on the rag died miserably—they didn't even have any clue what had happened. All they felt was how heaven and earth collapsed.

Even the few people who were aware of what happened weren't capable of resisting in a battle of this caliber.

The boundary wall that could only be broken down by the Eternal Realm warriors' full strength grew weak under the impact.

Splash! Once the south of the Separate Amber Province sank, the ground was split into two—a crack that extended millions of miles revealed the scene in the chaos.

The negative pressure produced as a result then attracted the chaotic clouds nearby which then swarmed toward the crack.

While the creatures of the Separate Amber Province could only sit still and wait for death, the Oneness Sky Palace's members still held a glimmer of hope for life.

The weakest disciples of the Oneness Sky Palace present were now at the Other Shore Realm, free from the threat of chaotic energy.

But during the battle between Claire and the Grandmaster of Heaven, only a slight impact could cause them either death or injury.

"Everyone, run to the west!"

"If you get lost, head for the Pear Hill!"

"To the west! Go through the boundary wall!"

The initially indestructible boundary wall was now riddled with holes, no longer able to stop everyone from escaping.

Libby, Pearce, and the rest quickly organized the Oneness Sky Palace's disciples for smoother passage through it.

In the meanwhile, the disciples of the Bearing race, the Divine Farmer race, and the New Moon race all returned to their respective flying ships.

A battle of this level had already completely disrupted the initial plan, but so long as they made it to the Pear Hill, survival wasn't impossible.

All the while, Claire was occupying the Yellow Thearch's body. The Divine Farmer had just been freed from a goat monster's state, and Mahoney had died. They had no time to worry about the lives of the Holy Soul Realm warriors.

Splash! Another crack appeared on the ground as thousands of clods were thrown into the sky—each clod was as huge as over a hundred mountains.

In one of the clods, a two-winged earth dragon was curling up. Once it felt movement from outside, it quickly came out of the clod, only to find it was already high in the sky.

Although it had reached the True God Realm, it wasn't all that intelligent— while it was still thinking hard about what exactly was going on, a flame shot toward it.

When the flame was still dozens of miles away, the heat it emitted had instantly burned the earth dragon through and through.

The Grandmaster of Heaven didn't want Othniel behind him to be any hindrance, so he simply stuffed him into another spatial treasure, the Fishing Drum. The two of them displayed incredible flexibility in a series of battles.

While Claire had occupied the Yellow Thearch's body through the eyeball, her strength wasn't affected in the least—she held no disadvantage in the face of the Grandmaster of Heaven.

"Grandmaster of Heaven… This is the second time I've fought with you, isn't it? It doesn't seem like you've made any progress," Claire said with a mocking smile.

The Grandmaster of Heaven remained composed, but he was rather surprised.

In terms of real strength, he was at the Eye Spirit's level—after fighting each other several times, this point was already proven.

But while in the Element Spirit race, Claire was ranked third in terms of strength, a great gap remained between her and the Eye Spirit. At least, the Grandmaster of Heaven wasn't taking her seriously back then.

In just a few chaotic eras, she had managed to grow so strong, exceeding his imagination.

Whoosh! While he was lost in thought, Claire used Zen to swing at him once again.

It had to be noted—in this state, Zen was an absolutely perfect weapon.

He had already managed to restrain several of the Grandmaster of Heaven's trump cards—he was a highly specialized weapon that could absorb all sorts of energy. Most importantly, it was impossible to damage him.

Thanks to Zen, the Grandmaster of Heaven was stuck in a passive situation.

After obtaining their freedom, Fuxi and the Snake Goddess flew to the southwest of the Separate Amber Province and stayed put.

"I thought I was the strongest in the chaos, but these two really are quite surprising…" Fuxi said resentfully, watching both Claire and the Grandmaster of Heaven up in the sky.

"They've lived through over a thousand chaotic eras. Of course, you can't even think of comparing yourself with them," remarked the Snake Goddess calmly.

The Nihility race, the Element Spirit race, and even the Snake Goddess were determined to get their hands on Zen. Now that their strength proved to be unequal to the task, they had to rely on a good strategy.

And while the Grandmaster of Heaven and Claire were distracted in battle, they had a chance.

As for the Black Ship, the captain wasn't watching the battle unfold.

If the Grandmaster of Heaven was defeated, the Black Ship would be doomed. Therefore, the captain merely had to wait for the result.

After all, he had something far more important to take care of.

Buzz! Another two Descending Rings were activated.

Then, two members of the Nihility race appeared before the captain.

One turned out to be Samantha, the Grandmaster of Heaven's disciple, and the other was the Evil God.

The latter glanced at the members of the Black Ship before snorting dismissively.

To that, the brass man's face immediately darkened. "Do you have something to say?"

The members of the Black Ship were not to be underestimated, after all.

It was with the Black Ship's help that the Evil God could grow so fast, get rid of Zen, and enter the Other Shore.

But he'd become rather supercilious soon after getting strong.

"Just leave him alone. He was cocky enough when he was weak," Shera said, smiling at the Evil God.

The Evil God smiled right back at her as though they were good friends that hadn't seen each other for a time.

It was because of Shera that he could stay on the Black Ship—she had proven to be greatly patient.

"Where is the incarnation of the evil will?" Samantha chimed in and broke the tension.

"Come with me," said the captain, nodding at Edith.

Once Edith stretched out her hands, an invisible space ship enveloped everyone. The next moment, it appeared in the west of the Separate Amber Province, where the Pear Hill and the Bearing race had first fought.

As the Divine Farmer chased the Invisible Ship, he consumed far too much of Usman's power, leaving the latter very weak.

Fortunately, he was bound to the Separate Amber Province. So long as it wasn't completely destroyed, he wouldn't perish.

Buzz! The Invisible Ship descended.

All the members of the Black Ship, the Evil God, and Samantha appeared before Usman.

As the latter raised his hand, his gaze fell upon Shera and the Evil God.

From Shera, he could feel a specific kind of emotion that seemed to have something to do with him.

Looking at the arrogant Evil God, he saw a bit of himself.

"What do you want?"

With the group approaching aggressively, he knew something bad was about to happen.

But he didn't seem to feel a sense of belonging to the Bearing race. He was like a drop of oil floating in the water, impossible for him to join any kind of force.

If he was forced to join the Black Ship, though, he wasn't going to refuse.

"This is the incarnation of the Source World's evil will. You will swallow him," said Shera firmly, pointing at Usman.

At that, Usman was instantly shocked. He raised his head to look Shera square in the eye. He wasn't afraid of anything, not even the warriors at the Eternal Realm, but now, a cold shiver just ran down his spine.

Chapter 3873 Fusion Just when Usman was about to struggle, Samantha, who was standing next to him, waved her horsetail whisk gently on his body.

As the whisk touched Usman's face, he instantly felt his body become stiff all over.

He was desperately trying to utter a word, but even his mouth was paralyzed, unable to say a word.

"How to devour him? Do I just eat him up directly?" the Evil God said as he looked at Usman with a wicked grin.

Although the Evil God would not devour the human flesh, he was pretty satisfied with Usman.

The aura being emitted by Usman was almost exactly the same as his. That was why he thought that Usman was very suitable to be a part of him.

"Don't you have the ability to absorb one's soul?" Samantha asked in confusion.

"That's right. You just need to devour his soul," Shera added.

There was actually nothing wrong with devouring Usman's physical body, but the most important thing was to fuse with his soul by consuming it.

With that, Samantha reached out her hand towards Usman's forehead, and a ray of cyan light was released from her palm.

Unable to move an inch, Usman only felt a grueling gravitational force coming from Samantha's hand. His eyes rolled and his body trembled violently. Soon, his soul was gradually dragged out of his body.

Generally, one's soul would look the same as their physical body, and there were only a very few exceptions.

Usman's soul was one of them. His soul was very unique. It sort of looked like a cat with its fur standing on end and covered with soul thorns. As Samantha dragged it out, it started struggling insanely in her hand.

However, if his physical body wasn't able to escape from Samantha, then his soul would be much more helpless.

Whoosh! Samantha waved Usman's soul and quickly placed it on the Evil God's head, for it to be absorbed into his mind. In just a matter of seconds, Usman's soul was successfully integrated into the Evil God's mind.

Unexpectedly, as soon as Usman's soul fused with the Evil God, it struggled and even tried to take over.

However, Samantha didn't have any intention of helping the Evil God out.

Instead, she asked him to deal with it by himself.

"Will he be okay?" Shera asked curiously.

"Well, it depends on him. But he better sort it out quickly." Samantha shrugged her shoulders and didn't seem to care much about it.

Upon seeing the indifferent expression on Samantha's face, Shera also backed off.

In fact, even the entire Nihility race treated the Evil God and Usman with the same attitude. As the incarnations of the evil wills, they weren't destined to be faithful partners for their race.

Besides, the Nihility race just needed their identity, and it didn't matter to them whoever played the dominant role.

However, for Shera, it was a bit complicated. Previously, she was infatuated with the original Usman, and the two of them shared some memories. So, she had quite a mixed feeling as the current Usman's soul was given to the Evil God.

"We have already given so much to the Evil God. If he can't even deal with the recently reborn Usman, then we might as well support Usman instead,"

Samantha added.

Meanwhile, a sharp look of pain suddenly appeared on the Evil God's face.

The muscles on his face twisted constantly and gave off strange expressions.

After a few seconds, his eyes closed and all his movements stopped. He seemed to have calmed down already.

Then, after a short while, he finally opened his eyes. Something definitely changed as his eyes were as deep as the ancient wells.

"So, you won?" Shera was the first to ask.

Shera felt that the Evil God didn't really change physically, but many incomprehensible expressions were contained in his eyes this time.

Then, the Evil God moved towards Shera. He looked at her with a peculiar expression in his eyes. "I found some strange memories."

"What do you mean by strange memories?" Shera asked.

All of a sudden, the Evil God reached out his hand, touched Shera's face, and drew her straight black hair towards him. As he smelled it, there was a visible frown on his face and he said, "There's a strong stench of corpses.

Why does that guy find it fragrant?"

"W-why do you have his previous memories?" Shera stuttered as she quickly stepped back. Her pale face turned a little red.

The other members of the Black Ship who were present eventually realized what was going on, but were also confused as to why it happened.

Usman often did that to Shera in the past. He loved her scent even though it smelled like corpses. But it was obvious that the Evil God didn't like that smell.

"When I merged with his soul, I also found some of the memory fragments.

I guess the current Usman wasn't aware that these memory fragments existed within him," the Evil God explained.

With the appearance of the incarnation of the evil will, the memories of his previous life should have completely disappeared. Even in the Source World, that was how they viewed reincarnation because the Memory Flame had completely vanished.

However, it seemed that some memories from the previous life of Usman were somehow carried on. And now, even the current Evil God had them.

"Well, it doesn't matter. What's important is how much impact you will have on the Source World," Samantha butted in.

To be able to control the Source World was equivalent to controlling the core of the chaos. This was also how other Eternal Realm masters thought.

But of course, it was no easy task to control the largest primitive land in the chaos.

Moreover, there had never been an incarnation of the primitive land, so they thought that theoretically, it was impossible to gain control of it.

However, many primitive lands had the incarnations of evil will. Take the one in Zen's body as an example. It was so small, but the Evil God still appeared.

The Black Ship and the Bearing race intentionally cultivated the incarnations of the evil will for the same purpose. They wanted to control the Source World through them.

"My impact on the Source World, huh?"

The Evil God's eyes narrowed as he looked at the boundary wall not far away.

After he devoured Usman's soul, he instantly felt that the broken boundary wall was somehow related to him.

Without wasting any time, the Evil God stretched out his hands towards the boundary wall.

Suddenly, the amber crystal clear boundary wall began to flow like melted honey.

Under his control, the boundary wall that stretched for hundreds of miles quickly collapsed and flowed steadily.

Seeing this, the other members of the Black Ship, including Shera and even Samantha, were greatly shocked.

After the previous Usman's appearance, he was carefully cultivated by the Black Ship.

At that time, Usman told them that he felt there were five stages that he could attain to improve himself.
